Foreign Important News

Various Attitudes of Countries After the US President's Declaration 43

Germany Overjoyed Beyond Words, Britain and Italy Expressed Willingness to Accept, France Felt Like a Bolt from the Blue, Japan Was Unwilling to Clearly Express Opposition

Facilitating European Economic Recovery, the World Market Suddenly Shows Vigor

United Press, 21st, Rapidan (Virginia) - Today, Sunday, US President Hoover is resting at this summer resort, pleased to see the enthusiastic response at home and abroad to the proposal to suspend war debts for one year. It seems that all European countries except France are happy to accept this proposal. However, the Paris government has informally stated that if Germany's unconditional reparations to France are also suspended, France will seriously object. As for the US Congress, President Hoover now believes that it will not be difficult to pass. Editorials in American and other newspapers have expressed great approval for this, especially in Britain. London believes that this plan will lead to the abolition of all war debts and the conclusion of a common agreement to help the world's economic recovery. It is expected that on the day of the successful conclusion of next year's disarmament conference, there will be an agreement to abolish war debts. The Germans are overjoyed about this, as if they have encountered the Winter Solstice. The German government originally had a plan to request a three-year suspension of reparations payments, but now it has temporarily abandoned it and formally expressed its willingness to formally accept the US President's proposal, but on the condition that it does not hinder future amendments to the Young Plan. It is now believed that this move can greatly consolidate the Brüning cabinet and prevent the spread of communist propaganda. The Italian government has expressed its willingness to accept this plan.

Reuters, 21st, Berlin - Tonight, the German government decided to accept President Hoover's proposal. Hoover, after deciding to help Europe and Germany, received a telegram from German President Hindenburg stating Germany's perilous situation, saying that if Germany continues to bear the burden of reparations, this situation will be unimaginable. He asked the US President to help quickly, or it would be too late.

Reuters, 22nd, Berlin - Yesterday, German political and financial leaders were extremely pleased after hearing President Hoover's proposal and felt a great weight lifted off their shoulders. June 21st will forever have commemorative value in German history because the suspension plan arrived at the most urgent time, averting financial collapse, otherwise, the whole world would have a very serious reaction. German Foreign Minister Curtius issued an article last night saying that the German government has notified the United States that it has gratefully accepted President Hoover's proposal. Germany can obtain a relief of about 75 million pounds. He also said that the possibility of revising the Young Plan will not be affected by the suspension measures. It is expected that Britain and Italy will soon announce their support for the US President's proposal, but France's attitude is more difficult to say. France seems to have made a sacrifice because France should receive 40 million pounds from Germany, while its war debt obligations are only 20 million pounds, so France will lose 20 million pounds. However, he does not believe that France will reject cooperation between Europe and the United States.

Reuters, 22nd, London - British Prime Minister MacDonald and Chancellor of the Exchequer Snowden both did not want to comment on President Hoover's plan to suspend debt payments yesterday, but it is expected that MacDonald will make some remarks on this matter in the House of Commons today. All British newspapers, regardless of faction, unanimously welcomed the US President's proposal.

Reuters, 21st, London - The profound impression created by President Hoover's proposal in Britain is not limited to the upper classes. People in the streets, trams, and buses, who usually do not read newspapers much on Sundays, are today vying to read the Washington telegrams reported in the newspapers. Reuters reporters visited various important figures in and out of office, many of whom said that this is the best news in many years. Overseas Territories Minister Thomas said that the US President's proposal is the first and essential step in the world's recovery, showing that the United States has recognized that no country can be independent of other countries. Liberal Party leader George was also very pleased and said that in 1922 he had a suggestion to cancel all international debts. If it had been implemented earlier, today's blow would not have occurred. US Treasury Secretary Mellon is currently in England visiting his son at Cambridge University and does not want to comment on this matter, saying that the situation is complicated and this trip is of a private nature, but he has been able to contribute something, but he is not in a position to say what aspect he has contributed to at the moment. As far as war debts are concerned, Britain has to pay the United States about 33 million pounds a year, while Britain can collect a total of 33.35 million pounds in war debts and reparations a year. France pays the United States about 7 million pounds a year, and Italy pays the United States about 4 million pounds a year. It is estimated that Germany has to pay a total of 80 million pounds a year. The British Cabinet will meet on Thursday to consider President Hoover's proposal. The French Minister of Finance has been studying this matter all day with financial experts and the President of the Bank of France.

National News Agency, 21st, Berlin - Whether the US President's plan to suspend debt payments for one year includes the unconditional annuity in German reparations is a question that has now caused disagreement between Germany and France. The French side said that the annuity is not within the scope of suspended reparations, while the German side said that all suspended reparations and war debts should be treated equally. The basis of the German argument is the official announcement of the United States, which clearly states that "the conditions for suspending all debts are that all debts owed by governments to governments and to major creditor countries are suspended for one year."

Political Program of the Chinese Kuomintang 44

Article 6 of Domestic Policy: Confirm that the people have complete freedom of assembly, association, speech, publication, residence, and belief.

Article 4 of Domestic Policy: Implement universal suffrage and abolish class elections based on property standards.

Articles 7 and 8 of Domestic Policy: Strictly define the statutory amount of land tax and prohibit all surcharges such as "鑒金" (mirror money), etc., which should all be abolished.

Article 12 of Domestic Policy: Affirm the principle of equality between men and women in law, economy and social, and promote the development of women's rights.

Article 9 of Domestic Policy: Investigate household registration, reorganize cultivated land, and adjust the production and sales of grain to ensure sufficient food for the people.

Since the US official announcement has repeatedly mentioned all debts, all debts, whether conditional or unconditional, are included in the suspension.

Reuters, 21st, Paris - Today, a semi-official statement said that the importance and generosity of the American action are admirable, but responsible parties in Paris believe that the suspension plan must be compatible with the Young Plan. The authorities of various countries do not need to exchange opinions before an international conference can be held. The date of this meeting has not yet been decided.

Reuters, 22nd, Paris - French newspapers believe that the suspension of debt payments originated from internal American charity because America's special interests do not allow German finance to collapse. The Paris Echo said that the French government hopes that President Hoover will not consider any actions that are detrimental to French interests. France cannot abandon the unconditional annual payment of 300 million francs that France should receive under the Young Plan. The Morning Post said that if President Hoover only says that the United States is willing to give up without forcing other countries to give up, then his actions will definitely gain infinite admiration. The Micro-Voice said that the suspension should be for a period of two years. The Exelsior said that the American proposal exceeds what France hopes for and even exceeds what France can concede. Humanité said that the arrival of the American proposal was like a bolt from the blue.

Reuters, 21st, New York - Most people regard President Hoover's announced proposal to suspend war debts as the most hopeful statement made by any head of state in the past decade. Newspapers have reported this news in large print. Although no newspapers have editorials, there is no doubt that public opinion will agree. Young, the creator of the Young Plan, who hopes to be the Democratic presidential candidate, said that the United States has spoken through its president and all parties support it as it should. This proposal is not only an act of clear creditors but also a beneficial statement from a large democratic country. He hopes that other governments can also act in this way. Once credit is restored, private interests will also benefit. To seek world prosperity, wisdom, courage, and goodwill are indispensable. He extremely approves of President Hoover's actions.

Reuters, 21st, New York - The New York Times' Washington correspondent said that since President Hoover has proposed a plan to suspend debt payments, there may be steps to reduce British debt interest rates. Now the domestic securities interest rate has a downward trend. The interest rates on the first and fourth liberty bonds, from 3.5% to 4.5%, will all be redeemed on January 1, 1932, and new bonds with lower interest rates will be issued. Since the interest paid by the United States is lower than before, it seems that the British debt interest rate cannot be uniquely high.

Reuters, 22nd, Washington - Senator Borah commented on President Hoover's proposal to suspend debt payments for one year, saying that if military spending is greatly reduced and reparations are reorganized within a year, then the world's great recovery can follow. Otherwise, extending the debt payment period will be of no help.

Page 8

Reuters, 21st, Vienna - Austrian Deputy Prime Minister Dr. Schober said that President Hoover's move to suspend war debt reparations for one year will be the starting point for true peace in Europe and the world in general.

Reuters, 21st, Geneva - The League of Nations welcomes President Hoover's proposal to suspend debt payments for one year, believing that this move will have a far-reaching and beneficial impact on the European Economic Alliance and is not only a good omen for the Disarmament Conference.

Reuters, 21st, Beijing - The Belgian National Daily reported that the US President's proposal will result in a net shortage of 580,000,000 francs for Belgium, so this proposal must be closely studied.

National News Agency, 22nd, Tokyo - Japanese Ministry of Finance officials today expressed their agreement in principle with the US President's proposal to suspend war debts for one year. However, Japan's situation is different from that of European countries. Japan has no war debts to the United States, and the 1931 budget already includes 6.3 million yen in German reparations. Therefore, it is uncertain whether the suspension proposal can be passed in the Japanese Diet. Japan fully agrees with President Hoover's fundamental plan to release the world from the heavy burden of war debts and promote economic recovery. However, before the government officially expresses its position, it is still necessary to carefully study the impact of the American plan.

Reuters, 22nd, Tokyo - A Japanese government spokesperson said today that there are two main reasons for the current global recession: one is the excessive burden of military spending, and the other is the concentration of cash in the United States and France. If the US President's proposal is accepted, it will greatly improve the prospects for the next Disarmament Conference because the United States can say at that time: "The United States has already helped to alleviate one of the major causes of the recession. The other cause should be cleared by European countries."

Reuters, 22nd, Tokyo - Japanese newspapers have not yet commented on President Hoover's proposal, but Mori Ken, who has held important government financial positions, published an interview with the Japan Public News Agency, saying that this proposal will have a good impact both materially and psychologically to curb the current economic downturn and can make capital flow more easily. It can temporarily avoid the inflow of cash into the United States. Although Japan has little direct contact, it can also benefit to some extent. He believes that the US President's move can re-ignite the discussion of the entire issue.

Reuters, 22nd, London - Today, the stock market opened with a new atmosphere. All securities rose in price due to the US President's proposal. Young bonds have risen from 66 to 74.5.

National News Agency, 22nd, Berlin - After the announcement of the US President's suspension plan, the stock exchange market here this morning suddenly became brisk, and the prices of all securities were much higher than the closing prices on Saturday. There was a lot of trading within a few hours of the opening, and it is feared that the number of transactions today could set a new record. On this day of financial panic, this phenomenon is indeed not easy.

Reuters, 22nd, Tokyo - Today, the prices of various securities on the stock exchange were firm and trending upward due to the US President's suggestion to suspend war debts for one year. This morning, the cotton market was also very active, and the forward prices were very high, which has not been seen for months. The silk market also has a rapid upward trend. Rice prices have also risen.

News

Central Party and National Government Memorial Week 45

Central Party Headquarters - At 9:00 am on June 22nd, the Central Party Headquarters held the 117th Memorial Week in the Great Hall. Central Committee members Kong Xiangxi, Ding Weifen, Chen Guofu, Fang Juehui, Wang Boling, Miao Peicheng, and staff from various departments and guests, about 500 people, attended. Ding Weifen presided. After the ceremony, Kong Xiangxi reported on the key points of the Provisional Constitution regarding people's livelihood: (1) Introduction: Because the primary task of construction is people's livelihood, the chapter on people's livelihood in the Provisional Constitution is very important. This chapter clearly declares the guidelines for people's livelihood construction, which can be divided into four points: 1. Focus on encouraging and assisting production. 2. Focus on developing agriculture. 3. Focus on cooperation between the government and the people (i.e., state-owned and private enterprises are equally important). 4. Focus on labor-capital coordination. (2) Encourage and Assist Production: Foreign industries are developed but there is inequality between rich and poor, so now we focus on distribution. China's industry is backward and people's livelihood is poor, so we should focus on production. Article 33 of the Provisional Constitution stipulates that the state should encourage and protect the people's production undertakings. However, how to protect and assist needs to be studied. (3) Development of Agriculture: China is an agricultural country, different from industrial and commercial countries, so it should first seek to develop agriculture. Article 34 of the Provisional Constitution stipulates that various intentions are very clear, among which three things should be paid special attention to: 1. Promote the warehousing system, based on the ancient Chinese three-warehouse system (community warehouse, support warehouse, and constant price warehouse), to promote its development with a spirit of mutual assistance. 2. Develop agricultural finance. Improving agriculture first lies in promoting financial institutions to enrich its funds, and agricultural banks and farmer banks should be equally important. 3. Reclamation of wasteland. Military and industrial reclamation should be organized by the state, and people's resettlement should be encouraged by the state and carried out by private individuals. (4) Cooperation between Government and People: Developing state capital is solid the policy of the party. However, private enterprises should also be encouraged. Articles 33 to 37 of the Provisional Constitution stipulate in detail that the government should carefully plan the production plan during the tutelage period, just like Russia's five-year plan, to ensure that the country's capital and labor are productive. (5) Labor-Capital Coordination: On the one hand, seek cooperation from labor, such as working hours and wages, should not only seek benefits for labor. On the other hand, attention should be paid to labor welfare undertakings, assisted by capitalists and the state to promote various facilities related to labor welfare. (6) Conclusion: The provisions on people's livelihood in the Provisional Constitution only represent the first step of the guidelines and plans for people's livelihood construction. In the future, during the constitutional period, the second and third steps will be gradually realized to complete the legacy of the Premier. In short, the Premier's Three Principles of the People and the Industrial Plan are very extensive in their announcement of principles and implementation procedures. Although the chapter on people's livelihood in this Provisional Constitution is based on this, it is actually a strategy that meets the requirements of the times during the tutelage period. If it can be implemented one by one, the first step in the people's livelihood problem can be solved. After the implementation of the Provisional Constitution, the responsibility of the party is even greater. It is hoped that various important policies regarding people's livelihood construction will be actively carried out with the greatest determination and effort. The people will be fortunate. After the report, the ceremony ended at 10 o'clock and dispersed.

National Government - At 10:00 am on the same morning, the National Government held the Premier's Memorial Week. Yu Youren, Shao Yuanchong, Ye Chucang, Zhu Peide, Kong Xiangxi, Ma Fuxiang, Liu Shangqing, Niu Yongjian, He Yaozu, Zhu Luhe, Lin *, Chen Shaokuan, Chen Yi, Wang Jiazhen, Ru Yuli, and staff from the National Government's civilian, military, and accounting departments, more than 300 people, attended. Yu Shiren presided. After the ceremony, Shao Yuanchong reported on the application of the examination system and the preparation of the recent examination. The words are generally as follows:

According to the Premier's plan, the five-power system will only be implemented when the constitutional government begins. Later, the central comrades felt when the National Government was reorganized in the seventeenth year that although the full implementation of the five-power constitution should be in the constitutional period, the five-power system itself should also have a relatively appropriate period of testing in order to give the content of the system a full understanding and accurate experience. Therefore, when the National Government was reorganized in the seventeenth year, it was decided to establish five courts to separately manage the five powers of administration, legislation, justice, examination, and supervision. The Examination Yuan went through more than a year of preparation time and was formally established in January last year. The work on the examination part is the responsibility of the Examination Committee. Since its establishment, it has been more than a year. During this period of more than a year, although many examination undertakings have not been directly carried out, on the one hand, the examinations separately held by the central government and various localities due to factual needs must be reviewed and guided. At the same time, there is also a very active preparation for the actual examination work. However, in the past year, because the examination laws and regulations have not been completed, the work has focused on the compilation of laws and regulations, the investigation of the examination system, and the organization of examination methods. It was not until the spring of this year that the National Government announced that the first higher examination would be formally held in the central government from mid-July, and the Higher Examination Assistance Office was established from mid-June to start handling registration and other preparations. Now, I will briefly talk about a few important points. (1) Examination Qualifications: The current examination law stipulates the qualifications of candidates. There are five clauses in Article 5. In addition to the provisions of the first clause "graduated from a national or established public or private university, independent college, or specialized school and obtained a certificate," the second clause "graduated from a foreign university, independent college, or specialized school recognized by the Ministry of Education and obtained a certificate," and the fifth clause "after passing the ordinary examination for four years or having served as a commissioned officer or a position equivalent to a commissioned officer for more than three years," there are two alternative methods, namely, the third clause stipulates "those with academic qualifications equivalent to those of a university or specialized school who have passed the qualification examination," and the fourth clause stipulates "those who have confirmed professional academic skills or works and have passed the review" can apply for the higher examination. Because there are such regulations, in the past few months, on the one hand, the central government and various provinces and cities have separately held qualification examinations. Anyone who has not formally graduated from school and feels that he has the ability to apply for the higher examination can first take the qualification examination to test the basic subjects of the university. After passing the qualification examination, he can apply for the higher examination. At the same time, a Higher Examination Professional Qualification Review Committee has been established in the Examination Committee. Anyone who has not graduated from a university or specialized school but has confirmed professional academic skills or works only needs to submit his professional works and achievements. If the review passes, he does not need to take the qualification examination first and can directly apply for the higher examination. (2) Examination Location: Our original plan was to divide the country into several regions. Whether it is the higher examination or the ordinary examination, it will be held separately in each region. However, this year, due to the difficulties in various equipment and the conditions in various localities, we cannot hold it in various parts of the country at the same time. At the same time, because the current examination method is neither entirely the method of the imperial examination in China in the past nor entirely the examination method of foreign countries, but is a new system created based on the legacy of the Premier. There are always some shortcomings in a new system in the initial implementation period, so it cannot be handled on a large scale. Therefore, it has been decided that the first higher examination will be held in the capital. Because the capital is the location of the National Government and is also the political center of China, holding the first higher examination in the capital can also make the people of the whole country have a deeper understanding of the location of the central government. (3) Examination Period: This examination is scheduled to be held in the very hot summer. This is due to factual issues. Because the Examination Yuan's preliminary examination hall plan has not yet been built due to the difficulty of construction costs. If the examination is to be held, it is impossible not to borrow schools or other public institutions. To borrow school classrooms or other buildings, it must be held during the summer vacation. Therefore, we know that it is very inappropriate to hold the examination during the summer vacation, but in order to realize the government's policy, we have to reluctantly do so. (4) Examination Procedure: Whether it is the higher examination or the ordinary examination, it is divided into three procedures. The first test is Chinese and the Three Principles of the People of the Chinese Kuomintang. The second test is a subject test, divided into compulsory subjects and elective subjects. Anyone who takes that kind of examination should take the compulsory subjects of that kind of examination, and the elective subjects are more specialized subjects in various examinations, which can be selected by the candidates from the listed subjects. Only after the average score of each subject taken in the first and second tests is passed can the third test be taken. The third test is an oral test, which is an oral inquiry on the compulsory subjects and experience of the candidates. (5) Types of Examinations: The types of the first higher examination are 1. General administrative personnel 2. Diplomatic officials and consular officials 3. Educational administrative personnel 4. Financial administrative personnel 5. Police administrative personnel. The reason why we only hold these five types of examinations is that on the one hand, the government agencies are in more urgent need of these five types of talents, and it is also to enable the appropriate and needed people obtained in this examination to do appropriate and needed work. (6) Examination Organization: The organization of the examination is divided into three parts. First, the work of assisting the examination: the preparations for the examination and all temporary affairs are almost all handled by the assisting part. The second is the internal work: the direct work of the examination is handled by the Examination Committee. The basic work of the Examination Committee is to review the qualifications of the candidates, formulate the examination questions for each subject, read the test papers, evaluate the scores, and finally announce the list of successful candidates. The work of the examination is very important, and contact with the outside world should be completely isolated. Therefore, the staff handling the examination, from the chairman of the Examination Committee, the members of the Examination Committee, the members of the Assisting Examination Committee, to the staff of the Secretariat of the Examination Committee, should be completely accommodated in the internal hall during the examination period and should not go out until the examination is over. Third, in order to ensure the strict confidentiality of the examination, the Examination Yuan should consult with the Control Yuan to appoint monitoring committee members when holding the examination. These monitoring committee members are appointed by members of the Control Committee or commissioners and are supervised by the monitoring committee members for various tasks inside and outside the field to show seriousness. After the report, the meeting was dismissed.

Successive Labor Strikes in Tianjin 46

The Yuyuan Cotton Mill's Labor Strike Reaches a Stalemate, Party and Government Agencies Are Unable to Mediate, and 30,000 People Will Lose Their Jobs If the Mill Closes

Tianjin Correspondence: Labor strikes have occurred frequently in the past two or three months, which is indeed a negative phenomenon in society. First, there was the waterworks labor strike, followed by the Hai River labor strike, as well as the Kai, Qi Xin, and Yaohua Yuda labor strikes. The workers have achieved considerable victories in all of these. Yesterday (the 18th), there was also a labor strike at the Yuyuan Cotton Mill. The general situation has already been telegraphed to the reporter. This morning at 8:00 AM, I took a car to Xiaoliuzhuang to investigate and record the situation as follows:

Motives for the Strike: The Yuyuan Factory is very large, with a total of four factories. The first, second, and third factories are for spinning yarn, and the fourth factory is for weaving cloth. Each yarn factory is divided into sections for spinning, fine yarn, winding yarn, and beating cotton. The wages of the winding yarn workers are lower than those of any other yarn factory, so on the 11th, they elected six representatives to negotiate directly with the factory manager, requesting a wage increase. The factory manager, Zhang Wanli, was peaceful and sent personnel to investigate other factories such as Beiyang, and learned that the winding yarn wages were lower than other factories, and immediately accepted the workers' request to be in line with other factories. This was originally a good intention on the part of the factory, but it unexpectedly triggered a cyclical labor strike. The fine yarn workers saw that the winding yarn workers had achieved victory and could not remain indifferent, so at 6:00 AM on the 18th, just as the night shift was ending and the day shift was starting, they suddenly shut down the machines in the first and second factories. The night shift workers could not leave the factory, and the day shift workers could not enter the factory. The situation was very tense at the time. The factory immediately reported to the Public Security Bureau, the Municipal Party Department, and the Social Affairs Bureau by telephone. The Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched a pistol squad, a security team, and a special affairs team to suppress the situation and guard the front and back doors of the factory. The order was slightly restored. In the afternoon, the Public Security Bureau dispatched the Sui Ning armored car to the factory to deter them.

Party and Government Mediation: After receiving the report, the party and government agencies believed that the Yuyuan labor strike had no warning signs before, but now it has suddenly occurred, fearing that there is a background. The Municipal Party Department sent Mr. Wang Hui, the Social Affairs Bureau sent Zhang Jinshi, and the Public Security Bureau sent Lu Lü one after another to the factory to investigate. It was only then that they learned that the motive for the strike was still simple. They then enlightened the workers, saying that a request for a salary increase should be submitted to the factory by the trade union in writing, listing the reasons, and at the same time, it should be reported to the party and government agencies. If the factory does not accept the conditions, the party and government agencies can come out to mediate. A strike can only be carried out if mediation fails. However, this time, it was not requested by the trade union, nor was it reported to the party and government agencies, and no written statement was submitted to the factory. A sudden strike is not in line with the procedures. But now that things have come to this, please elect representatives for consultation. Unexpectedly, the workers were afraid that the elected representatives would be dismissed in the future, and no one came forward to negotiate, resulting in no results. At 3:00 PM, Wang Junhui and others went to the factory again to explain the pros and cons, and still asked them to elect representatives for negotiation with the factory, otherwise there would be no solution. As a result, the workers still shirked responsibility and no one was willing to take responsibility as a representative. Wang Junhui and others then consulted the factory's opinion, and the factory's attitude was very firm, believing that the factory's wages were not lower than other factories. If the factory's business is profitable, a wage increase is not a problem, but now it loses hundreds of thousands of yuan every year. If the workers cannot understand and are forced to close down, it is also impossible. Wang Junhui and others felt that the matter was very difficult and declined to mediate.

The Attitude of Capital: According to factory manager Zhang Wanli, the factory's capital is 5.6 million yuan, of which the Okura Foreign Firm has 2 million Japanese yen. At the time of borrowing Japanese debts, the Japanese yen exchange rate was very low, and 100 yuan of national currency was equal to 75 Japanese yen. Now, more than 240 yuan of national currency is equal to 100 Japanese yen. This loss alone is no less than 3 million yuan. In addition, raw materials have risen in price, output taxes are heavy, and debt interest rates are high, while sales prices are low, resulting in annual losses of 400,000 to 500,000 yuan. The reason for not immediately stopping work is that the unemployment of more than 5,600 workers is worrying, and we have to survive. The factory cares for the workers and has a clear conscience. For example, on the 11th of this month, the winding yarn workers requested a wage increase. The factory immediately sent personnel to investigate and found that the wages were indeed lower than other factories, and immediately increased them. Unexpectedly, the fine yarn workers saw that the winding yarn workers had achieved victory and wanted to follow suit. They did not know that the average daily wage of the fine yarn workers is more than six jiao. Not only is there no such high wage in other yarn factories in this city, but even in Shanghai, where the cost of living is the highest, it is only like this. Therefore, the factory cannot accept this request, because the factory cannot afford it. Even if we take a step back and reluctantly accept their request, the coarse yarn, cotton beating, and weaving workers will inevitably ask for the same. If the factory does not accept it, there is no excuse to explain it. If we accept it, we cannot afford it. Moreover, the strike by the fine yarn workers has exceeded the normal track, so we hope that the workers will realize and resume work, and not be used by a few bad elements. The factory believes that this strike is unreasonable and illegal. The factory is not responsible for the wages during the strike period. Moreover, the strike by the first and second factories (about 1,300 to 1,400 people) has affected more than 4,000 workers in the third and fourth factories who cannot work. These more than 4,000 workers have suffered the loss of wages in vain. Isn't it too unfair? The factory, in order to care for the majority of workers, intends to dismiss a small number of bad elements and allow the remaining good workers to resume work. In case a small number of bad elements hold the entire workforce hostage and force the factory to be unable to exercise its powers, it will have to listen to them. If other events unfortunately occur in the future that affect social order, the factory cannot be responsible. This intention has been stated to the party and government.

Announcement of Shutdown: Yesterday, the party and government agencies were in a stalemate because the labor and capital sides were tending to extremes and could not be mediated. They all returned empty-handed. The Public Security Bureau, in view of security concerns, ordered the Tuchengzi Police Station in the rural area to dispatch two large bicycle pistol squads and one company of security guards to strictly guard the factory wall, and also dispatched police to guard the watchtowers at the four corners. The factory's labor inspection section posted a notice of shutdown last night, saying: "The A and B shifts of the fine yarn department of the first and second factories are on strike and refuse to leave the factory, and the entire factory is in a state of shutdown and cannot start work. Please be informed of this. Yuyuan Textile Company Inspection Section respectfully informs, June 18."

The Attitude of Labor: The initiators of this strike are the fine yarn workers of the first and second factories. After going to work (night shift) on the afternoon of the 17th, the foremen generally held a meeting and said that prices are now expensive and the wages we receive cannot maintain our lives. The factory union does not ask for the workers, so we have to unite ourselves and ask the factory manager directly. We will not resume work until we achieve our goal. Look at the winding yarn workers who have not been requested by the union and have directly requested and have been victorious. We should work hard together and we will definitely achieve our goal. So at 5:30 AM on the 19th, when the night shift workers were leaving, they blocked the machines in the first and second factories and declared a strike and occupied the factory and did not disperse. At 6:00 AM, the day shift workers went to work one after another, but they could not enter the factory to work. It was not until noon that they dispersed. These more than 1,300 night shift workers declared that they would not agree to a salary increase and vowed to die in the factory. Among them, there were more than 400 female workers. Because of all the inconvenience, they left the factory and went home to wait for a solution. These 800 to 900 workers did not eat yesterday (the 18th). Today (the 19th), the families of the workers heard the news and began to send food to the factory. Today, there is persuasion to go home and think of a solution. The workers still said that they would rather die than leave the factory and advised those who did not participate in the strike to act in unison. However, those who did not strike were afraid that the stalemate would lead to no good results, so they were very hesitant.

The Silence of the Trade Union: The reporter also went to the Yuyuan Trade Union. According to the directors and supervisors, the basic daily wage of the fine yarn workers is 48 cents. In the early years, there were bonuses for work. For example, each person should spin a certain number of yarns per day. If they spin more yarns, they would get a bonus. At that time, each person could earn 60 cents a day. In recent years, in order to reduce costs, the factory has been spinning second-class raw materials into first-class yarn, so that the machine's ability cannot be matched. Although the workers work 11 and a half hours per shift without a minute of rest, the output is still difficult to meet the quota, so the bonus for daily output surplus is eliminated invisibly. The factory is dissatisfied because of the reduced output, and the workers have suffered losses because of the reduced output, so this time they requested an increase of 9 cents for each day's work, and the workers requested an increase of 5 cents for each day's work. This request was not reported to the union, and the procedures were improper. The union sympathizes with the workers' demands, but is really dissatisfied with their actions. Now there is no way to persuade them to resume work, and there is no basis for asking the factory to accept the workers' demands, so we have to remain silent for the time being. However, we hope that both labor and capital will compromise so that work can be resumed as soon as possible. We also hope that those on strike will realize that otherwise, if the factory is forced to close down, not only will more than 5,600 workers lose their jobs, but the unemployment of those who indirectly rely on the workers for their livelihoods will be no less than 20,000 to 30,000 people. (June 19)

South Manchuria Urges Resolution of Steel Rail Payment for the Jilin-Changchun Railway 47

The Case During Wei Wuying's Tenure

Shenyang Correspondence, Republic of China, Year 17: Wei Wuying, the former director of the Jilin-Changchun Railway, believed that the Jilin-Changchun business was developing rapidly, and the number of trains and weight were increasing. The original 60-pound steel rails had too weak a load-bearing capacity, and he feared that it would cause congestion in the train. He decided to purchase 80-pound steel rails. The 60-pound steel rails that were replaced were sold to the Jidun Railway for laying branch lines. The purchase price of the 80-pound steel rails was borrowed from the South Manchuria Railway Company in accordance with Article 18 of the Jilin-Changchun Railway Loan Agreement. When originally reporting to the Northeast Transportation Committee, it was said that these steel rails were ordered from the Hanyang Iron Works, but after the approval, it was not known why the decision was suddenly changed to purchase from the Japanese merchant Mitsubishi Corporation. The acceptance was not carried out in accordance with the statutory chemical inspection procedures, and the South Manchuria Company had already advanced more than 900,000 Japanese yen to Mitsubishi Corporation when the goods arrived. At that time, Wei was preparing to report the reason for changing the purchase location and the situation of negotiating a formal loan agreement with South Manchuria when the investigation event occurred. Wei left his post in a hurry, and this case became a double dispute internally and externally. Internally, it was suspected that Wei did not purchase from the Hanyang factory but purchased from Japanese merchants without authorization, and the acceptance was not carried out in accordance with the statutory procedures. It is difficult to predict whether old rails were used to fill the number, so this case has become a major issue in Wei's unfinished handover of the Jilin-Changchun and Jidun Railways. Externally, the case of Wei involved the issue of interest. According to Wei's letter to South Manchuria, before the loan agreement was established,

Page 9

News Briefs 48

The advance payment was calculated at an annual interest rate of 9%. Now, because we do not recognize Wei's change of the original plan, we also deny Wei's recognition of the advance payment interest. Although the Japanese side has repeatedly urged us, we always replied by saying that the dispute has not been resolved. However, in fact, these steel rails have long been laid, and the Japanese advance payment has long been allocated, so the Japanese side's urging to calculate this interest or revise the formal contract cannot be said to be without considerable reason. Therefore, the authorities intend to first negotiate with South Manchuria to reduce the interest rate during the advance payment period, and then revise the formal contract for resolution. The original letter from South Manchuria to the Jilin-Changchun Railway Bureau is recorded below: "The case shows that your bureau previously purchased 80-pound steel rails from Mitsubishi Corporation, and our company advanced the price, totaling 1,182,058.74 Japanese yen as of April 5 of this year, with a calculation sheet attached. Please check and pay. Your bureau's letter stated that the Mitsubishi steel rail case has not yet been resolved, and all interest amounts must be settled and paid after the resolution. It is difficult to recognize the principal and interest. This case is the price of steel rails purchased by your bureau from the local Mitsubishi Corporation. Our company temporarily advanced the payment at the request of your bureau. The method of organizing the advance payment should be carried out in accordance with Article 18 of the Loan Agreement until the goods arrive at your bureau to conclude the loan agreement. If the loan agreement is not established, your bureau owes our company. The debt must also pay a certain interest rate. Recently, our company has repeatedly requested payment of the price and interest. It can be asserted that the interest amount in this case should be calculated according to a certain interest rate. In this situation, your bureau should immediately pay the debt or conveniently perform the procedure of concluding the loan agreement, choose one of the two. Please do not delay. Attached is the calculation sheet as of October 6, Showa 5, totaling 1,131,156.69 Japanese yen for the principal, and 50,902.05 Japanese yen for the interest from October 6, Showa 5 to April 5 of this year, totaling 1,182,058.74 Japanese yen." (June 18)

Negotiations on the Fuzhou Bridge Project 49

Japanese Industrial Company Unable to Complete Construction as Agreed

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Jiangnan Wanshou Bridge in Minyuan spans the north and south banks of Taijiang and is the transportation hub of the entire city. In November of last year, when Jiang Pingfan was the acting director of the Construction Department, it was agreed to rebuild it by introducing Tamura Teijiro, the Japanese Consul in Fujian, to contract the Taiwan Daiwa Industrial Company (an engineering company temporarily organized by the Japanese) to renovate the steel-bone cement bridge deck. The agreed project cost was over 190,000 yuan, and the deadline for completion was June 10 of this year. If the project was not completed by the deadline, the company would have to compensate the Chinese government for a loss of 100 yuan per day (the daily ferry cost during the renovation period is 300 yuan). However, only one-fourth of the project has been completed by the deadline. The provincial government is preparing to ask the Japanese Consul, but the company said that the reasons for the delay in the bridge project were: 1. The Chinese supervisors arbitrarily picked on the materials and projects; 2. The subcontracted Chinese workers did not listen to the company's command. The Japanese Consul, instead, proposed five conditions to the provincial government: (1) Extend the deadline by three months; (2) Waive the overdue compensation fee; (3) Add additional subsidies; (4) Withdraw the official supervision; (5) Urge the subcontracted Chinese workers. The provincial government has not yet responded. However, the merchants and people in Guanyin Well in the south of the bridge, Zhongting Street in the north of the bridge, and Zhongzhou Street in the middle of the West Bridge have suffered losses in business since the two bridges were renovated and cut off traffic for half a year. If they are allowed to delay with excuses, the merchants and people will suffer even more. They have specially organized a bridge project negotiation support association to request the provincial government to negotiate seriously with the Japanese Consul, detain the representative of the Daiwa Company and order them to compensate the merchants and people for their losses. On the other hand, they will settle the account with them and deduct the amount due for the completed part of the Jiangnan Bridge. The remaining amount should be returned immediately so that our country can re-recruit workers to build the bridge. (June 19)

Anhui Province Establishes a Narcotics Suppression and Investigation Office 50

Hao Zihua Talks About the Reasons for Establishing the Office

Bengbu Correspondence: Regarding the issue of narcotics suppression, the authorities have determined a new plan. The Narcotics Suppression Committee will establish narcotics suppression and investigation offices in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Anhui, Jiangxi and other provinces. The Anhui Narcotics Suppression and Investigation Office was established in Wuhu a few days ago. The office is divided into three sections. Hao Zihua, the director, has sent many narcotics suppression committee members to various counties to investigate the actual situation of narcotics poisoning, depending on the needs of the locality, in order to establish narcotics suppression and investigation sub-offices. It has been decided to establish them in seven places: Anqing, Datong, Bengbu, Hefei, Chuxian, Fuyang, and Hao County. Hao Zihua arrived in Bengbu from Wuhu at 10:00 AM yesterday (20th) to establish the Bengbu Narcotics Suppression and Investigation Sub-Office, and appointed Yao Xingqiao as the director. The office is located at the Yuelai Company in Hexia. The internal organization is divided into three shares, and the staff will start working within a day. According to Hao, the new narcotics suppression plan of the Narcotics Suppression Committee is to gradually move from a slow ban to a strict ban. The ban should be completely banned within six years from the 20th year of the Republic of China. Within six years, the narcotics suppression measures will be changed each year according to the circumstances, and the ban must be banned within the time limit. The Narcotics Suppression and Investigation Office will proceed step by step according to this guideline. The initial work is to start with an investigation of opium smokers. How many young people are there in each county or port? The absolute ban on smoking is absolutely prohibited. Patients and the elderly are registered separately, and a registration fee is collected monthly for a limited time to ban them. If the ban is taken strictly, smokers will not only be in danger of life, but morphine, Jindan, white powder and other drugs can take advantage of the opportunity to harm them even more. There will also be considerable bans on the trafficking of opium. If the opium collected by the planting households this year is not allowed to be sold or even found and burned, the planting households will suffer great losses, which is also unreasonable. Therefore, a considerable ban is still outside the ban on collection. However, the detailed regulations on narcotics suppression and investigation have not yet been issued by the Narcotics Suppression Committee. However, it is heard that the local party departments are still opposing it. (June 21)

A suicide case occurred here yesterday. It turned out that a young military officer surnamed Wang was having an affair with a woman surnamed Hu in Huaxing Street. Unexpectedly, the affair was not secret and was detected by Hu, who severely reprimanded his wife. The wife then committed suicide by swallowing opium. The young military officer thought that he had caused Bo Ren's death and also bought arsenic and liquor and went straight to his tomb. The Tianzhu Church in Wuhu has the highest annual rental income from real estate outside the church in the whole county and has a tendency to manipulate real estate. The county government previously reported to the provincial government that it had gone beyond the scope of preaching and was preparing to take it back in accordance with the regulations. However, the church has unreasonably resisted for days and sent a letter to the county government requesting understanding, causing great indignation among the people of the county. All groups have now organized a committee to recover real estate outside the church to assist the government in its implementation and vow to achieve the goal.

Kunshan 52

The Wu kidnapping case has rescued two hostages. Wu Yunzhou, a merchant from Xiema and Heshangbang, and his niece, a woman surnamed Xu from Zhangpu, were kidnapped by bandits last month. Wu Shaokang of the investigation team went to Shanghai to arrest Zhou Ermazi, the bandit leader in the case, and eight other bandits, including Lü Er'er. They were sent to the county government for interrogation and confessed to the kidnapping of Wu. Wu's captain in Shanghai, together with the Yidaojiao Security Group, continued to arrest a bandit named Wang Yuting and rescued the two hostages surnamed Xu. Songjiang 53

The Headquarters Executed Bandits by Shooting. The Provincial Security Second Group and the Songjiang-Jinshan-Jiading Bandit Suppression Headquarters previously arrested Zhang Yisheng, a bandit who robbed the Jin Siniang Bridge, Feng Chengu, and Feng Meiquan's home and kidnapped them. The bandit was escorted to the Headquarters by Bai Jizhi, the battalion commander of the First Battalion, for interrogation and confessed to robbery and extortion. He was sentenced to death and reported to the Jiangsu Appeasement Superintendent's Office, which ordered him to sign and escort the prisoner to the execution ground for execution by shooting on the morning of this (22nd).

Bidding for the Feces Removal Contractor: The First District Office of the County Public Security Bureau intends to present a case to the Sanitation Office in the city and town to standardize the removal of feces and ban open-air pit toilets, and submit it to the county government for approval by the department. According to the Shanghai feces removal method, the city and town are divided into five roads to recruit merchants to contract. The central road is limited to 400 yuan, the southwest roads are 300 yuan each, the east road is 200 yuan, and the north road is 150 yuan, based on the size of the population. The contractor builds a manure pool and hires people to remove the feces from house to house every morning and gives a small amount of manure money. However, since there are many applicants for this business, it has been decided to announce a tender and publicly open the tender at the First District Office on the 24th of this month to show fairness.

Suzhou 54

Robbery and Injury in Taiping Village, Puzhuang: Zhang Xunru's home in Taiping Bridge Village, two miles away from Puzhuang, was robbed by eight bandits at 1:00 AM on the 20th, and more than 100 yuan of silver dollars were taken away. Before leaving, they cut off Zhang Xunru's left arm and fled towards the direction of Mu Tu.

County Magistrate Huang Resigns to the Province: Huang Yunzhen, the county magistrate of Wu County, resigned to the province three times due to old age and fatigue. The provincial government retained him and gave him seven days of leave. After receiving the order, Huang went to Shanghai by car at noon on the 22nd to recuperate. The county affairs were temporarily handled by Secretary Mei Huang.

Wuxi 55

Business Tax Collection Deadline: The Jiangsu Provincial Government previously resolved to implement the collection of business tax on April 1st and decided that the entire industry would acknowledge and pay taxes separately, ordering the business tax bureaus of various counties to earnestly comply. Wuxi has repeatedly convened business tax bureaus to jointly invite various industries with the county Chamber of Commerce to determine the amount of tax to be acknowledged on a daily basis. It has been determined that there are a total of fifty-eight industries with an annual tax payment of approximately 50,000 yuan. On the 18th, County Magistrate Pan, Business Tax Bureau Director Yang, and Chamber of Commerce Chairman Qian went to the provincial government and finance department to report the tax amount determined by each industry and personally explained the particularly difficult situation of the Wuxi commercial sector this year due to the silk market. Chairman Ye and Director Chen of the Finance Department agreed to allow a trial run for the determined industries this year, and all industries that have not yet been determined should establish a review committee to conduct a thorough re-examination and be handled by the bureau in a separate case, all to be collected quarterly and the collected taxes should be reported and remitted steadily. Now the Business Tax Bureau has followed the provincial order to notify the fifty-eight industries that have already been determined to pay the first quarter's tax payment before the 26th of this month for reporting and remittance. All industries in urban and rural areas that have not yet been determined are limited to actively contact and acknowledge payment within five days in order to achieve consistency. As for the starting date of collection, the Chamber of Commerce has strived to negotiate with the province, and it has now been agreed that when paying the first quarter's tax payment, the month will not be temporarily noted on the receipt, and will be handled in accordance with the general plan after the entire province makes a decision.

The Romantic Affair of the Deputy Director of the Second Public Security Bureau: Sun Rongding, the deputy director of the Second Public Security Bureau outside Guangfu Gate in our county, has recently had an ambiguous relationship with Miss Tang Quanyu, a top student of a certain sericulture school, seemingly like husband and wife. The day before yesterday, Sun (alias Han Wei'an) and Miss Tang went to the Jingtai Inn on the road to open room number five for a secret meeting. This matter was discovered by Zou Tingliang and Wei Mei, two residents of the county, who immediately and quietly rushed to the inn, knocked open the door, and caught them both. Director Sun of the bureau, knowing that things were not going well, immediately asked Zou and Wei not to publicize the matter and then called a friend to the inn to mediate, which led to a settlement. After this incident occurred, it spread throughout the city, and everyone regarded it as gossip.

Robbery in Judong Township: Criminals Caught on the Spot: Yesterday (the 22nd) at 0:30 AM, more than ten robbers suddenly came to the homes of Zhuang Yinbao and Zhuang Zhenxiang, residents of Wucun Village, Judong Township, Shitanwan, District 16 of the county. They spoke with a northern accent and broke into the house with electric batons, robbing them of about 200 silver dollars worth of silver coins and clothing, with the Zhenxiang family suffering greater losses. After the 34th Detachment of the Shitanwan Township Business Corps learned of this, Coach Nie Pengren led more than 20 armed corps members to chase them separately. They caught two robbers, Tang Kejiao and Zhang Zhiyuan, near the city, and recovered a top hat, sixteen padded and cotton-padded single clothes, and two strings of grain from Zhuang Zhenxiang's home, confirming that they were the robbers. They were immediately brought to the Business Corps Association and transferred to the county court for interrogation.

Public Security Bureau Director Suddenly Arrested: County Magistrate Pan Zhongjia received a secret order from the Nanjing Garrison Headquarters the day before yesterday, ordering the arrest of Fu Qin, director of the 13th Public Security Bureau of the 5th District, and his transfer to Beijing for investigation. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Pan immediately ordered Director Xu of the County Public Security Bureau to handle it. After receiving the order, Xu immediately notified Director Fu of the bureau to come to the bureau for a discussion. Li Ashou's Tragic Death Relief Association: Li Ashou, a carpenter who collected waste from the Ye Qin yarn factory outside the East Gate, went to the Yongyu Silk Factory outside the South Gate the day before yesterday to deliver food and was severely beaten by factory guard Wang Yucheng, rickshaw driver Song Ada, and others. On the same day, representatives of the entire county's labor community held a relief meeting in the former Labor Association and resolved the following important cases: (1) The Li Ashou Tragic Death Relief Association of the Wuxi Labor Community was named; (2) Appoint Hui Jizhi from the Silk Factory Industry Employees' Union, Sun Xiangfeng from the Newspaper Occupational Union, and eight others as executive committee members; (3) Demand that the court arrest Wu Xilin, who instigated the murder, provide compensation to Li Ashou's family, and punish Wang Wei, the negligent director of the Third Bureau, who disregarded human life; (4) Appoint Gui Wochen as a standing committee member; (5) Hire lawyers An Ruotai and Tang Ying as legal advisors to be responsible for the lawsuit and send telegrams to the national labor community for unified assistance.

Changzhou 56

Chamber of Commerce Chairman Resigns Due to Business Tax: The Wuyi County Chamber of Commerce held a meeting of industry leaders at 2 PM on the 21st to discuss the business tax recognition amount, as a final negotiation was required. Representatives from 31 industries, totaling more than 60 people, attended. Chairman Guo Cifen also attended despite his illness. After the meeting, the Chamber of Commerce first reported the details of the negotiations with the Business Tax Bureau one by one and advised each industry to automatically increase the recognition amount in order to reach a satisfactory resolution. Each industry requested that the agreed recognition amount for industries that had not yet been recognized last time be increased. If more than 30,000 yuan can be raised, unlisted industry shops and village towns, totaling approximately 50,000 or more, will be added. However, most of those who have not recognized the amount cannot determine the recognition amount due to brokerage fees and exemption requests. At this point in the discussion, County Magistrate Zhang, due to the provincial government's telegram urging collection, brought the telegram to the meeting and earnestly persuaded each industry, but each industry still declined to increase the amount. Chairman Guo persuaded each industry to make an effort to increase the recognition amount by 20%. Many representatives of each industry were dissatisfied. Chairman Guo declared his resignation on the spot and withdrew from the meeting. County Magistrate Zhang again persuaded each industry to make an effort to agree, and the representatives had no choice but to stand up and pass the recognition amount. As a result, the recognition amount of each industry increased by 20%, totaling 24,000 yuan. Industries that have not been recognized will be handled directly by the Business Tax Bureau.

Young Grandson of the Zhou Family in Qianbugou Kidnapped: At about 9 PM the night before last, five bandits, each with guns, suddenly broke into the home of Zhou Dasan, a farmer in Qianbugou, the Tenth District of the county, and kidnapped Zhou's four-year-old grandson. It is heard that Zhou has reported to the township office and forwarded the report to the county government for strict investigation.

Verdict on the Bone Steaming and Examination Case: Xia Yuzhu, a farmer from Xiajiaji in the Tenth District of the county, filed a complaint with the county government last month together with his father-in-law Liu Hengshun, accusing his elder brother Xia Meilian and others of strangling his wife, Xia Liu. The county government conducted a major bone steaming and examination at the Qigong Temple last month. The result of the examination revealed that Xia Liu was injured before her death and committed suicide by hanging herself. Now it has been ruled that the defendants Xia Meilian and Xia Zhu were each sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the crime of injury causing harm to Xia Liu. The number of days of detention before the final verdict will be offset at a rate of 200 days to one day. The defendants Zhang Danian and Yin Zhu were found not guilty.

The Zhou Changxing Family Robbed by Bandits: The Zhou Changxing family in Zhoujiazhuang, Nianziqiao, in the eastern countryside of the county, was suddenly visited by three bandits on the night of the 19th, each wielding iron bars and other weapons. Establishment of the Temple Property Education Promotion Association 62

Cai Yuanpei Discusses the General Situation of the National Peiping Library 63

Created by Combining the Former Peiping and Beihai Libraries

Collection of More Than 400,000 Volumes of Chinese and Western Books, Extremely Grand and Magnificent

Recently, the National Peiping Library is about to be completed. The reporter believes that it is of great importance to Chinese culture, so he specially visited Cai Yuanpei, the director of the library. According to the investigation, the library was originally created by combining the former Peiping Library and the Beihai Library. The former was funded by the Ministry of Education. The existing collection includes 36,300 volumes of the Siku Quanshu from Wenjin Pavilion, 8,000 volumes of Dunhuang scriptures, more than 160,000 volumes of general books, more than 22,000 volumes of rare books, 8,600 volumes of Tang dynasty handwritten scriptures, more than 100 volumes of Xixia scriptures, as well as the Yongle Encyclopedia and many fine books from the Cabinet. The latter is a part of the China Cultural and Educational Fund's business. The current collection includes more than 75,000 volumes of general books, more than 6,000 volumes of rare books, and more than 150 kinds of complete science magazines. In addition, about 40,000 volumes of Western books have been collected. In June of the 18th year, the Board of Directors of the Cultural Foundation decided to combine the two libraries into the National Peiping Library, which is affiliated to the Ministry of Education. The Ministry of Education appointed seven directors to be responsible for the library and appointed Cai as the director of the library and Yuan Tongli as the deputy director. Later, the old site was too small and not suitable for library use, so the Ministry of Education was requested to approve the allocation of funds from the Boxer Indemnity to build a new library on the old Royal Horse Garden in Peiping, covering an area of more than 100 acres. Construction began more than two years ago. The construction cost is estimated to be more than 600,000 yuan. The construction project was handed over on the 20th of this month and the completion ceremony is scheduled to be held on the 25th. The building of the library is completely in the palace style, and the walls are decorated with glazed dragons, which are very rich in oriental colors. The library is in the shape of the Chinese character "工" and has three floors. The front part is for reading and the back part is for storing books. The first floor is for geography, the second floor is for general reading rooms, and the third floor is for observing rare books. The library faces Beihai to the east, and the scenery of Beiguang Mountain can be fully enjoyed. There are dozens of acres of open space in front and behind the library, planted with evergreen trees, making the air particularly fresh. The internal facilities are extremely magnificent, and the book storage is made of steel bones, making it the only large library in the country. It will inevitably make a great contribution to China's future culture and academics. Cai has decided to travel north tomorrow (22nd) to preside over the opening ceremony and attend the standing committee meeting of the China Cultural and Educational Foundation Committee.

Ministry Order to Remedy the Charter of the Changsha Middle School Student Self-Government Association 64

The Ministry of Education, according to the report from the Hunan Education Department, stated that the charters of student self-government associations at all levels of schools, in accordance with Article 21 of the Central Promulgated Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline and Item 6 of the Social Organization Organization Procedures, should be approved by the local senior Party Department and reported to the competent authorities for record. However, recently, the charters submitted by the student self-government associations of various secondary schools in Changsha City for registration are inconsistent with the Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline promulgated by the Central Government. If they are all filed for record, there will inevitably be obstacles in the future. If they are amended, the Party Department has already approved the implementation. What should be stipulated to prevent malpractices? It is reasonable to submit a request for instructions. The Ministry of Education ordered that the charters of student self-government associations in various schools, if they are inconsistent with the Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline promulgated by the Central Government, should still be discussed by the competent authorities and the local senior Party Department to remedy the situation in order to comply with the regulations, even if they have been approved by the Party Department for implementation. Furthermore, the "competent authorities" mentioned in Article 21 of the Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline, in accordance with Article 2 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Student Self-Government Association Organization Outline, are the county government in the county and the city government in the city. If the draft charters of the student self-government associations of various secondary schools in Changsha City are reported to the department for record, they should all be rejected. Furthermore, the Social Organization Organization Procedures mentioned in the report have long been abolished. All Social Organization Organization Procedures have been incorporated into the Amended People's Organization Program passed by the 101st Standing Committee of the Central Committee and notified in the Ministry's Order No. 786 last August. This is for your information.

Chinese Economic Society Establishes Essay Competition Award Money 67

The Chinese Economic Society Essay Award Money Regulations are as follows: (1) The society has established essay competition award money to encourage economic academic research; (2) The total amount of the award money is temporarily limited to 500 national currency; (3) The award money is divided into four awards: one first prize of 300 yuan, one second prize of 100 yuan, and two third prizes of 50 yuan each; (4) Essay topics can be chosen independently, but must be limited to the following areas: (a) Silver price and currency system issues; (b) Economic policy and economic design; (c) Labor-management coordination; (5) The essay must be the author's personal research result. If other people's opinions or materials are cited, the reference source, book title, and page number must be indicated; (6) The essay must be written in Chinese, using new punctuation marks, in either classical or vernacular style; (7) There is no fixed limit to the number of words in the essay, but it must be at least 10,000 words; (8) Contestants should submit their name, address, and topic to the secretary of the society's board of directors (Zhu Binyuan of the Economic Committee of the Legislative Yuan) before August 10, 2020, to be forwarded to the society's essay committee; (9) The deadline for submitting essays is October 30, 2020. Late submissions will be invalid; (10) The essay competition judging committee will be organized by the society's board of directors by inviting experts.

Jinan University Especially Emphasizes the Spirit of Research 74

Establishment of a New Economics Research Association

Jinan University bears a particularly important and great mission. Merely reciting textbooks and repeating what others have said is certainly insufficient to fulfill the task of national construction. At the morning memorial week ceremony, President Zheng Hongnian reported that in the future, special emphasis should be placed on the spirit of research. In addition to the gradual establishment of research departments in each college, the research direction should be as follows: (1) The Nanyang-Americas Culture Department must cooperate and connect with the Business College's Commercial Investigation Department, the Law College's Political Economics Department, and the high school's business courses, introducing all overseas Chinese affairs to the country and all domestic economic conditions, market changes, academic hygiene surveys, news of educational and cultural institutions, and the creation of domestic products to overseas Chinese compatriots at any time. (2) We should study practical knowledge. Simply discussing high-level theories is still not applicable. For example, the Department of Diplomacy and Consular Affairs should delve into the evolution of diplomatic precedents, especially the process of China's treaties with various countries over the past eighty years, carefully study and distinguish who is an imperialist, and formulate how to deal with them in the future in order to open a new era in the diplomatic world. (3) In addition to expounding research insights in ordinary academic theories and common sense, the publications of various colleges and departments must pay attention to the development and improvement of the department. In addition, new books and magazines should be purchased at any time to catch up with new academic developments. (4) Collect important materials related to the national economy, enrich teaching materials, and provide them for domestic workers engaged in the construction of new economies, and hire specialized scholars to establish a new economics research association (according to this association, the plan is very large and has been approved by the school's administrative meeting yesterday).

Recent News from the Business School of National Central University 76

Since the Business School of National Central University in this city moved into its newly built school building in the spring, the scale has been grand, the facilities have been thorough, and the curriculum has been enriched. The college is worthy of being the highest institution of higher learning in the country. It is heard that the college is scheduled to begin its summer vacation on the 23rd of this month. Recently, teachers and staff have been extremely busy with semester examinations and graduation examinations, and even did not take a break on Sunday. The examination affairs will not be completed until the 22nd. It is heard that the school usually places great emphasis on academic credits. This time, only Shi Zemin, Jiang Zhilin, Ge Dingbang, Huang Zhongying, and four other students will graduate. Those whose credits are insufficient will be left to take the examinations in the next semester, which shows the high level of the school's students. Furthermore, the school will begin enrolling new students on July 7th. Recently, application letters have been pouring in from all over. President Xu Peikun is deeply concerned that there will be too many students in the next semester and that the original dormitory will not be sufficient for accommodation. Therefore, he has devised a method to set up another off-campus dormitory near the Water and Electricity Road, which is currently under construction and will be completed before the start of the autumn semester for accommodation. In addition, the school has always had extremely strict examinations for new students, such as economics, bookkeeping, logic, and oral examinations, which are all major subjects. However, this year's recruitment of new students will be held simultaneously in Guangzhou, Beiping, and Wuhan, and there is deep concern that the levels in various places will be uneven and that the economic and other subjects will not be prepared in time. Therefore, the school has decided to temporarily cancel these subjects to benefit the students, but after the new students are admitted, they must still complete the study of each of these courses before they are allowed to graduate.

Unprecedented Plunge in Gold Speculation 87

Impact of US Suspending Debt Payments

Plunged by 65.6 Taels

Rising Silver Prices Also a Major Factor Yesterday, the 22nd, there was a sudden and drastic change in gold speculation, with an unprecedented drop. From morning to noon, there was a difference of more than forty taels, and in the afternoon there was a fluctuation of twenty-six or seven taels. The final plunge of more than sixty-five taels was truly unexpected. The situation changed rapidly, with fluctuations of ten taels or more being commonplace, making it difficult for traders to cope. It was almost like a thunderbolt. The reasons for the terrible drop were that the United States had decided to allow a one-year postponement for Germany's war reparations, and that overseas silver prices had risen for two consecutive days. Furthermore, the atmosphere was unfavorable, and major bulls such as Qian Changxiang, Bing Xing, Zhi Fengyong, and others bravely sold off due to environmental pressure. Only the bears saw a glimmer of hope, so the market opened low. Later, the wind and waves were treacherous, with a sense of mountain shaking and earthquake. There was a rapid decline, but a small rebound. Foreign exchange has been lengthened by one level, and the internal market is also very sluggish. By noon, it had suddenly broken 760 taels, and the market initially stabilized. However, it was still weak, with extreme fluctuations, hovering around forty taels. It once fell to 730 taels, and the exchange rate became even more loose, causing great terror. The final count was thirty-five or six taels. This phenomenon is likely to be dangerous in the future. The big market this morning should see a big rise.
