With Clear Weather, the Rice Market's Decline Becomes More Severe 94

Xin Zha. Yesterday, the weather cleared up, and shipments from various groups were still pouring in, with about 30 to 40 boats arriving, resulting in abundant stock. Market sales were sluggish, and people's sentiment was loose. The top-grade goods from Changshu and Xichong fell by nearly a "chi." The market lacked interest in previous transactions, falling by two or three "jiao," and the future direction is difficult to determine. Only by seeking new avenues can there be hope for a turnaround. Transactions for "Yang Du Jian" were extremely few in the morning. Although arrivals were scarce, prices fell by a "jiao." There was little demand for "埠 Jian." The market for glutinous rice was extremely scarce here, and prices were difficult to reduce.

Hu Nan. Yesterday, about 30 boats arrived from the Huangpu River, and sales in urban and rural areas were stagnant. The wholesale price of top-grade "Hou Geng" from Changshu and Suzhou fell slightly by two "jiao." The overall trend was more peaceful than in Zhabei. The stock of goods from Tongli and Beixiang was not abundant, and the capacity of shops was limited. Prices for early rice fell by half a "chi." There was some demand for thin rice, but demand from Ningbo was still weak. There was also limited movement for selected high-quality rice in this area, and prices fell by a "chi." Arrivals and sales of "Yang Du Jian" were balanced, and the trend was sluggish. The "Bai Yuan" market experienced some changes, and the port was quiet. The market shape was stable.

Silk and Tea, the Precious Eyebrows from Northern Wu Have Already Opened 95

The "Zhen Mei" green tea from northern Wu, known for its excellent production methods in Wuyuan, had a large number of new samples displayed by teahouses such as Zhongxinchang, Hong Yuanyong, and Yong Shengchang yesterday, which attracted a lot of attention from British and French merchants. However, due to the recent price declines of teas from Tunxi and Suian, most merchants, while eager to purchase, had intentions to suppress prices. However, Chinese merchants, deeply aware of the poor harvest in the interior this year, adhered to the principle of "scarce goods are precious" and maintained an exceptionally firm attitude. Subsequently, Baocheng and other firms opened the first round of prices, ranging from 150 to 200 taels, which was 30 to 40 taels higher than last year for goods to the Northeast. The "Zhen Mei" green tea from northern Wu also opened at prices ranging from 70 to 90 taels, which was 20 to 30 taels higher than last year. However, there did not appear to be large-scale sales of goods from Tunxi and Wudong yesterday.

Russian Firm Begins Purchasing Qihong Tea 96

The Russian Assistance Association Foreign Firm, which sells a large amount of tea, began purchasing Qimen Hongcha yesterday and also started purchasing Gongxi items. The firm is also proceeding with estimations to procure Chinese tea. Chinese tea merchants' attitude towards this market trend has become firm.

The Trend of Piece Goods is Firm 97

Cotton Cloth from This Factory. The market has been rising continuously in recent days, especially with fine cloth frequently reaching new highs. "Lan Zunyu" is priced at 7 taels and 8.5 qian, "Labatong" at 7 taels and 8 qian, "Yanghe" at 7 taels and 7.5 qian, "Lan Feiyu" at 8 taels and 0.05, "Lan Ji" at 7 taels and 6.25 qian, and "Jixiang" at 7 taels and 6.75 qian, all of which are rare high prices in recent years. The dyed grey fabric from Sichuan is selling exceptionally well. Over 500 pieces of the "Lan Shuangyu" brand have been sold, resulting in a price of 7 taels and 5.25 qian, and "Yanghe" is priced at 7 taels and 6.25 qian. Spot goods for 9-pound coarse cloth are still around 5 taels yesterday. 11-pound cloth has risen slightly, with "Renzhong" at 5 taels and 4 qian, "Siping Lian" at 5 taels and 4.5 qian, and "Santou" at 5 taels and 5.25 qian. Coarse twill is difficult to rise due to limited sales.

Eastern and Western Piece Goods. The market situation remains firm. Although the gold market plummeted yesterday, people's attitude remained stable because the prices were still similar to before, considering the rise in the Three Products. The Sichuan group had the best sales yesterday. The most traded were "Zhi Gong Ni," with over 100 pieces sold at a price of 3 qian, 8 fen, and 2.5 li. "Si Junzi" sold for 3 qian and 3.5 fen. Fine " " Ancient City had a one fen increase. " " Ball" sold for 4 qian, and "San You Tu" sold for 3 qian and 4.5 fen. Bleached cloth all rose in price. " " Bridge" sold for 12 taels and 5 qian, "Fu Shou San Xing" for 11 taels and 1.5 qian, and "Ding Fu Jun" for 11 taels and 9.5 qian. "Santou Mao Si Bu" has opened at 3 taels and 3 qian, and common sales opened at 2 taels and 8.5 qian. "Zhi Gong Duan" all rose in price. "Tian Ci Cai Yuan" and "Tian Ci Huang Jin" both sold for 4 qian and 1 fen, and "Di Yi Gong" for 3 qian, 7 fen, and 7.5 li. The northern groups purchased quite a bit, and western goods remained scarce and expensive.

The Sugar Market's Price Fluctuations Follow the Sharp Drop in Gold Prices 98

Yesterday, the sugar market lacked telegrams from the producing areas. Apart from the guild's market marking prices, the weakening of the foreign exchange rate caused a weakening of public sentiment, and market prices suddenly trended downward. The transaction price for Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse white sugar was 11 taels and 5.5 qian, and high-quality TK brand was 11 taels and 6.5 qian, falling by 1.5 qian compared to before, and the market was also flat. There was also little demand for No. 20 medium white sugar at 10 taels and 0.09 qian. Japanese sugar fell even more sharply, falling by two qian compared to before. Strong N brand was priced at 11 taels and 1.5 qian, YT brand was 11 taels and 1.5 qian, TK brand was the same price, SH brand was 10 taels and 0.09 qian, J brand was 11 taels and 6 qian, YRO brand was 10 taels and 0.08 qian, YP brand was 11 taels and 5.5 qian, Taikoo B brand was 11 qian and 6.5 qian, and DY brand was 11 taels and 1.5 qian. Although trading was still active, the market appeared quite stable, and transactions in the listed markets were all quiet.

Local News

Tan Yunshan Returns from Travels to Tibet and India 140

After a few days of rest, he will go to Beijing to report, carrying Gandhi's message to Chinese youth.

The National Government previously sent special envoy Mr. Xie Guoliang, along with Mr. Tan Yunshan, the editor of the Burmese Chinese newspaper, to visit Tibet. They traveled through India, crossed the world's highest peak, the Himalayas, passed through Darjeeling, and after more than twenty days, finally reached Lhasa. They stayed for two months, taking the opportunity to observe various facilities. The mission was successfully completed. Besides planning to write travel notes for the public in the future, Mr. Tan returned to the country from India yesterday and stayed at a new business inn. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency specifically visited him at his residence. According to him, the trip to Tibet was extremely difficult. Along the way, there was ice and snow, dangerous mountains, and the climate was cold, often below zero degrees on the thermometer. The two traveled by horse. They often saw mules and horses frozen to death. Mr. Xie passed away midway due to old age and physical weakness. The scene was very tragic. Mr. Tan persevered and finally arrived in Lhasa (Western Capital), where he met the Dalai Lama, conveyed the National Government's intentions, and used this opportunity to strengthen connections. He was warmly welcomed, and all his missions were successfully completed. Afterward, he took the opportunity to visit India and tour various Buddhist holy sites and major cities in India. He, along with Liu Renhang, Liu Xiunan, Daoyi, Biguan, the two Dharma masters, Gao Jianwen, Yu Pingke, and Zhuang Xiquan, fellow travelers, investigated Buddhist sites. Places visited included Bodh Gaya, where Buddha attained enlightenment, Vulture Peak, where Buddha preached, Nalanda, where the Tripitaka Master obtained scriptures, Deer Park, where Buddha turned the wheel of Dharma, Kushinagar, where Buddha attained Nirvana, Lumbini, where Buddha was born, and Jetavana Anathapindika's Park in Shravasti, where the World Honored One taught the Dharma. Samkissa, where the Buddha ascended to preach to his mother for three months, the king, ministers, laypeople, and disciples waited to welcome the Buddha. All were famous holy sites. He also purchased photographs and Buddhist souvenirs. Furthermore, he visited Delhi, the current capital of India, and visited the palace, the New Delhi Parliament, the Governor's Mansion, and museums. He also met with Mahatma Gandhi in Bardoli, West India, and stayed with him for several days, deeply moved. Gandhi asked Tan to convey a few words to the Chinese youth: "Dear friends, you must come and see me again at your convenience. My advice to the Chinese youth is that China's salvation requires pure, impartial love and should not rely on force, which only hurts life." Mr. Tan previously served as a Chinese professor at the International University founded by the Indian poet Tagore. This time, he investigated Tibetan and Indian culture and religion, with many feelings. After a few days of rest, he will go to Beijing to report to the National Government and the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission. He also hopes to do his best to communicate Chinese and Western ethnic cultures and plans to co-found an Oriental Academy with Huang Renzhi, Huang Jingwan, Wang Yiting, Dai Jitao, and the Venerable Master Taixu.

Naval Recruits Passed Through Shanghai Yesterday to Go to Fujian 141

Led by Commander Gao Xianshen of the Tongji warship, the training fleet of the Ministry of the Navy, the Tongji warship set sail from Beijing the day before yesterday, carrying ninety-five newly recruited naval navigation and machinery students, including Wang Guogui, to the Mawei Naval Academy in Fuzhou for studies. They arrived in Shanghai at seven o'clock yesterday morning and docked at Wusongkou. A reporter from the Ri Ri News Agency went to Gaochang Temple yesterday, took a naval launch to Songjiang, boarded the ship, and visited Commander Gao Xianshen of the warship. He inquired about the examination process and other details. The details are recorded as follows:

Examination Process 142

In order to cultivate naval talents, the Ministry of the Navy recruited ninety-six new students in April of last year to study at the Mawei Naval Academy in Fuzhou. This year, another hundred students were recruited for navigation and machinery. Before being sent to the Ministry of the Navy, they were first recommended by the provincial governments and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. The provincial and municipal education authorities conducted an examination. Those who passed were graduates of higher primary schools or above. Those who passed were then sent to the Ministry of the Navy for examination. A total of 335 people were sent from various provinces and cities. Among them, about sixty people who were slightly inferior in physical examination and eyesight were not admitted to the examination, which was a pity. The examination committee strictly selected only ninety-four people. Wang Shousheng, a student recommended by Guizhou, was temporarily delayed due to the long distance. A supplementary examination was held and Wang Shousheng was admitted. In total, ninety-five people were admitted. On the morning of the 21st (the day before yesterday), at seven o'clock in the morning, they were led to board the ship at the Xiaguan Naval Dock in Beijing. The ship set sail at about eight o'clock and arrived at Wusongkou this morning (yesterday morning) at seven o'clock.

Waiting to Change Clothes 143

The Shanghai Naval Management Office had ordered student uniforms and leather shoes from a certain new clothing store. The clothing store transported the white drill uniforms and yellow leather shoes to Gaochang Temple for the students to change. The naval launch transported them to the Tongji warship at Wusongkou for distribution to all students. The exchanged casual clothes were stored or sent to the students' homes.

Student Age 144

The youngest student recruited this time was twelve years old, accounting for one-third of the entire team. The oldest was only fifteen or sixteen years old. They were all energetic, spoke fluent Mandarin, and were quite lovable. They also had no thoughts of being far from home, which made their ambition even more commendable.

Graduation Period 145

The admitted students first enter the school as recruits for six months, then formally attend classes for five years. After graduation, they practice machinery for one year, navigation for one year, and gunnery for one year, for a total of eight years before they are officially graduated. The best students are sent to Europe and the United States for further study to achieve greater accomplishments. However, during these eight years, students are not allowed to ask for leave to go home without reason, and there are no long vacations in the school.

Departure to Fujian on the Same Day 146

The ship arrived in Shanghai at seven o'clock yesterday morning (22nd). Because it did not stay long, it did not sail into the Gaochang Naval Dock, but docked at Wusongkou. In the afternoon, at about four o'clock, after all the students had changed into their uniforms, the ship set sail from Shanghai and sailed directly to Mawei, Fuzhou, to send the students to school.

Attitudes of the Wusong Chamber of Commerce After Being Taken Over 147

Various News

Wusong Chamber of Commerce Holds Meeting: Yesterday was the third day after the Wusong Chamber of Commerce was suspended. All members of the association went to the chamber around 10 o'clock the night before to discuss solutions. The majority advocated for striving to maintain its existence, otherwise, all businesses would automatically close. After the standing committee members Zheng Dong and Zhang Zengjie earnestly persuaded them, they telegraphed the Seventh District Public Security Bureau to send District Officer Cheng to the scene to dissuade them, and also dispatched police to maintain order, fortunately avoiding any incidents. Then, all members elected representatives to hold a discussion meeting. Zheng Shushan was temporarily elected as chairman. Subsequently, all matters were discussed and it was resolved to first telegraph the Ministry of Industry and the Municipal Government of the Executive Yuan to request instructions, and also send a telegram to all provincial, municipal, and county chambers of commerce and newspaper offices nationwide to request assistance. Wang Yingru, Zheng Shushan, and Shi Yunjie were publicly elected as representatives to go to Beijing by the early train this morning to petition the relevant authorities. If they cannot achieve their goals, they are willing to dissolve the chamber of commerce and oppose the establishment of a branch office. Regarding the debt issue of the association, creditors are first requested to come to the association to register. Yao Pan'an and Yang Jingbo were appointed to handle the registration matters. The meeting adjourned at 12 o'clock. The text of the telegram is recorded below: National Government Executive Yuan, Ministry of Industry, Shanghai Municipal Government, National Federation of Commerce, to all provincial, municipal, and county chambers of commerce and newspaper offices nationwide: Wusong is the gateway to the Yangtze River and the throat of Shanghai. On land, it is the end of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway; on water, it is the crucial point for entering and exiting the river and sea. Its position is truly the key to the Southeast and the linchpin of the entire country. Since the Ministry promulgated the Chamber of Commerce Law in the late Qing Dynasty, the town's merchants and residents have voluntarily organized the Chamber of Commerce for more than twenty years. In normal times, it resolves difficulties and disputes, and ship merchants from all provinces particularly appreciate its protection. In times of crisis, it mediates and protects the military and political circles, and also provides much assistance. In short, the small local group is truly something that relies on reality, not empty words. Unexpectedly, in May of last year, the Shanghai Business Consolidation Association, under the name of consolidating Shanghai merchant groups, approved the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau's reply, saying that Wusong is relatively close and there is no need to establish a special association. It is advisable to consider setting up a branch office and instructed the Wusong Chamber of Commerce to end its operations and hand over its affairs. Merchants and residents were greatly dissatisfied upon hearing this. Although they wanted to strive for survival, they always sought peaceful procedures to achieve their goals of making requests. Therefore, they went through the Municipal Association, the Municipal Bureau, and the great departments of the government, and their steps never dared to go beyond the bounds. They stated the reasons why they should not be reorganized and requested that the decision be withdrawn, and they appealed to the great departments to maintain their stance of striving for reasons, and they ultimately hoped to have a day of understanding. The views of the Chamber of Commerce members were exactly the same as those of all our merchants. Recently, we were fortunate to receive an instruction from the Ministry of Industry, stating that after reviewing the claims made by the association, there were reasonable grounds. We should wait for a factual report to be submitted to the Executive Yuan for review and instructions before issuing further orders. This order was on file. However, on the morning of the 20th of this month, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent Luo Qinghua, accompanied by Hu Yuqi from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and Jin Zhongjian from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, leading many armed police officers to the Chamber of Commerce. They announced the instructions, including removing the association's sign, confiscating seals, and sealing up files and public property. They specified each measure to be taken and demanded immediate compliance. At that time, standing committee members Zhang Zengjie and Zheng Dong, etc., informed them that the Chamber of Commerce had a reply from the Ministry of Industry, and immediately presented it for review. The reply said that although they should wait for the central government to resolve the matter, the orders from the Social Affairs Bureau were very strict and absolutely could not be delayed. The committee members also told them that the Chamber of Commerce is a group, so how could the transfer to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce be so solemn? We, one or two people, cannot be fully responsible. This was not allowed either. Therefore, the Wusong Chamber of Commerce, which has been in existence for more than twenty years, came to an end. I secretly think that even if the Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce do not talk about the Chamber of Commerce Law, they should also know that there is a central government. Even though they have seen the ministry's order, they still disregard everything. If the Social Affairs Bureau issues such an order, it is close to oppressing merchants and residents. If the Municipal Chamber of Commerce issues such an order, it is using force to unify merchant groups and cannot avoid occupying the position of a commercial warlord. Now, under the clear blue sky and white sun, may I ask, if the central government does not allow the Wusong Chamber of Commerce to exist, no matter what, there will be no resistance. Why use armed force to intimidate? The Chamber of Commerce can be deceived, and the merchants can be deceived even more. In the future, for any small and weak group in the city, what kind of freedom of power and what kind of legal protection will there be? Suffering this oppression, it is not difficult for our merchants to strike in order to have a corresponding treatment. I am afraid that the crime of coercion by the masses will soon arrive, and it will be contrary to the original intention of peaceful negotiations. Therefore, representatives were urgently elected to go to both Beijing and the city to make appeals and petitions. First, a telegram was sent requesting the esteemed Executive Yuan, Ministry, (esteemed association), (esteemed newspaper) to review the unbearable insults suffered by the Wusong Chamber of Commerce and quickly preside over justice and issue instructions to comply with (provide assistance and forward the telegram to all chambers of commerce nationwide to call for appeals together) so that it can continue to exist to avoid oppression and maintain the law and the group. The entire merchants and residents of Wusong Town, Shanghai City, Shi Yunjie, Zhu Shijun, Bao Zijing, Lu Damin, etc., one hundred and thirty-five people, respectfully kowtow.

News from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce 148

A reporter from the New Voice Agency specially visited Wang Xiaoqi, chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, yesterday regarding the Wusong Chamber of Commerce issue, to inquire about his opinions on future handling. According to his remarks, the original plan for Wusong to establish a branch office was decided by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. During the Shanghai Merchant Group Consolidation Committee, the 47th Standing Committee meeting discussed how to consolidate the Wusong Chamber of Commerce. The results of the day's discussion were based on Article 5 of the Chamber of Commerce Law, which states that "in prosperous towns, chambers of commerce may also be established independently or jointly," and Article 8 of the same law, which states that "chambers of commerce shall establish offices within their regions, and when it is deemed necessary due to special circumstances, branch offices may be established with the approval of the members' meeting." Wusong, as a prosperous commercial town, is actually qualified to establish both a chamber of commerce and a branch office. How should this be handled? It was resolved to send a letter to the Social Affairs Bureau for review in order to show caution. Subsequently, on May 17 of last year, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau's Reply No. 3774 was received, stating that the town had already been incorporated into the special municipal area and was located within the scope of the Municipal Area. The distance to your association is relatively close and transportation is also convenient. It seems that there is no need to establish a special association. It is advisable to consider establishing a branch office to integrate the organizational structure while enhancing commercial benefits. After receiving the letter, the Merchant Group Consolidation Committee again decided at its 50th Standing Committee meeting to forward the letter to the Wusong Chamber of Commerce, instructing it to immediately handle the conclusion and handover. The association would then decide on the establishment of a branch office at the Chamber of Commerce members' meeting. After the letter was sent, on June 10, a letter was received from the Wusong Chamber of Commerce stating the reasons why it should establish an independent chamber of commerce and could not be reorganized into a branch office. The Merchant Group Consolidation Committee again sent a letter requesting the Social Affairs Bureau to review it. Subsequently, on June 25, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's first members' meeting was held, and it was resolved to establish branch offices in Wusong, Qibao, Jiangwan, and Pudong. It was submitted to the Ministry of Industry and the Social Affairs Bureau for approval and record. The Jiangwan and Pudong branch offices have now been established. As for the Qibao branch office, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce received instructions from the Social Affairs Bureau that the Qibao Town area, according to the regional division designated by the province and city, is in the list of areas temporarily postponed for takeover by the Municipal Government, and the branch office should also be temporarily postponed for establishment. Therefore, although the Chamber of Commerce received requests from the merchants and residents of Qibao to establish it, it complied with the orders of the competent authorities and did not establish it. As for Wusong, it has been nearly a year since the Chamber of Commerce members' meeting resolved to establish it. The Chamber of Commerce has also not sent anyone to take over, as handling merchant groups is purely an obligation and there are no rights involved in the matter. It was not until April 27 of this year that the Chamber of Commerce received Instruction No. 9260 from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, forwarding the Municipal Government's order approving the Ministry of Industry's consultation that the reasons for the Wusong Chamber of Commerce to change its location were sufficient and should be approved as proposed and forwarded for notification. It was also forwarded to the Wusong Chamber of Commerce, requesting it to immediately comply with the order to conclude and prepare for handover. After the letter was sent, more than a month passed and the Chamber of Commerce had not received a reply from the Wusong Chamber of Commerce. It was not until the 16th of this month that the Social Affairs Bureau issued an instruction ordering them to send personnel to guide the reorganization of the Chamber of Commerce. If it continued to resist, it would be dissolved. The wording was extremely stern. Another letter was immediately forwarded to the Wusong Chamber of Commerce and Luo Qinghua, director of the Commercial Affairs Section, was sent to guide the reorganization in accordance with the order. While preparing to handle it, on the 19th, an urgent telegram was received from the Social Affairs Bureau stating that it had received instructions from the Municipal Government to urge them to go for takeover. Therefore, the next morning, Luo Qinghua, director of the Commercial Affairs Section, and Xue Guangqian, clerk, were sent, accompanied by the representatives of the Social Security and Public Security Bureaus, to handle the matter. Currently, the seals and stamps of the association have been examined and received by the representatives of the Social Affairs Bureau. The official documents and files have also been sealed and signed jointly by the representatives of the Social Security and Public Security Bureaus and handed over to the Chamber of Commerce for safekeeping. Therefore, the Chamber of Commerce handled this matter entirely in accordance with the orders of the competent authorities. As for how to handle it in the future, the Chamber of Commerce also knows very well that Wusong is located in an important area with prosperous commerce, and the Chamber's affairs cannot be allowed to be suspended. It was decided at a temporary standing committee meeting held today to submit a request to the Social Affairs Bureau for review. If it is approved to establish a branch office by the Chamber of Commerce, the Chamber of Commerce will carefully consider the candidates for the director of the branch office and will definitely select someone who is familiar with the Wusong business situation and can win the hearts of the people. In the future, all matters related to Wusong will be handled by the branch office at any time. More important matters that the branch office cannot handle will be transferred to the Chamber of Commerce for handling. If handled in this way, the Chamber's activities will not only be inconvenient, but its strength may be stronger than before. As for the debts owed by the former Wusong Chamber of Commerce, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce believes that those that are truly legitimate after review should be the responsibility of the Chamber of Commerce to sort out and repay.

News from the Social Affairs Bureau 149

A reporter from the Wuchen Agency went to the Social Affairs Bureau to inquire about the details of this matter. According to the person in charge, the bureau received an order from the Municipal Government two months ago to reorganize the Wusong Chamber of Commerce into the Wusong Branch Office of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce in order to comply with the laws and regulations. It ordered the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to guide the reorganization and instructed the former Wusong Chamber of Commerce to comply. After the instructions were sent, it had not yet complied. Now, it has received another order from the Municipal Government stating that the former Chamber of Commerce is still using the former name to the outside world, which is inappropriate. Therefore, personnel were dispatched to the Wusong Chamber of Commerce on the 20th of this month, together with the Public Security Bureau and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, to take over. If the Wusong Chamber of Commerce is allowed to exist, then the Nanshi and Zhabei Chambers of Commerce can also cite this precedent and request to re-establish themselves. All the reorganization work of the former Shanghai Merchant Group Consolidation Committee will inevitably become empty. The various trade and labor unions in the city will also inevitably split up, which will inevitably lead to disputes. The reporter also inquired about the aftermath. According to reports, the bureau has ordered the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to establish the Wusong Branch Office within ten days, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce will continue to handle all affairs. As for the debts owed by the former Chamber of Commerce, if they are indeed due to expenses, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce should be responsible for handling them.

The Third Shanghai County Representative Assembly, Day Three 150

Morning: Memorial Week and Fourth Meeting

Afternoon: Fifth Meeting and Closing Ceremony

The Third Shanghai County Representative Assembly has been held at the County Party Headquarters since the 20th of this month. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday was the third day of the assembly. The General Manager's Memorial Week was held at 9:00 AM, followed by the fourth formal meeting to discuss various proposals. From 1:00 PM, the fifth meeting continued and the declaration of the assembly was passed. The closing ceremony was held at 4:00 PM. The details of each item are recorded below.

Attending Representatives 151

Assembly Declaration 158

Shanghai County Third Representative Assembly Declaration: The Chinese Kuomintang, through the arduous creation of the General Manager and the sacrifice of countless martyrs, has finally achieved today's unification. However, considering the current situation, the Red Bandits are cornered in Xianggan, and the disputes in Guangdong are suddenly arising. The people's hardships have not been eliminated, and construction is also facing obstacles. How should our party comrades unite their spirits, concentrate their strength, follow the General Manager's legacy, and devote themselves to the construction during the period of political tutelage? On the day of holding the third county-wide representative assembly, I would like to propose the following five drafts to share with all the people and comrades of the county to go to one day to thoroughly abolish the unequal treaties. In recent years, with the joint efforts of the government and the people, although the unequal treaties will only be modified, considering the neighboring environment of this county, the concessions of various countries are still in place. Foreign warships are frequently docked in the Huangpu River. Although the voices of consular jurisdiction and inland navigation rights being revoked have been noisy for a long time, they have not yet been realized. This has harmed the development of our industry and commerce and hindered the completion of our national revolution. Our people should support the government in implementing the resolutions of the National Assembly and thoroughly abolish the unequal treaties in order to restore our country's inherent sovereignty. Secondly, support the peaceful unification of the country. Civil war is not only a painful and shameful thing, but also the country's vitality is hurt and the people's livelihoods are seriously damaged. Now the Guangdong incident was originally a party dispute, but unfortunately it has now appeared as a rebellion. The central government is fundamentally tolerant and intends to use political means to seek a peaceful solution, which is what our people hope for. This meeting will sincerely support the central government's advocacy of peaceful unification, and those who disregard the overall situation and deliberately disrupt peaceful unification will be abandoned by the people of the whole country. Furthermore, such as the Red Bandits who are wreaking havoc on the people, the central government is fully engaged in suppressing them. The day of clearing them is just around the corner. All our people should rise up to assist the government in completing the work of suppressing the Red Bandits in order to lay the foundation for the country. Thirdly, determine the policy for the county's party affairs. In accordance with the central government's regulations, the party affairs work plan during the period of political tutelage and the actual environment and time needs of the county have been reviewed. The Assembly has decided that the county's party affairs work plan will be implemented in one for social investigation. Most of the county is rural, and the majority of the people in the county are farmers, so special attention should be paid to the investigation of the rural economy, land, household registration, etc. Secondly, to investigate the general education level, local customs and habits, and the conditions of schools, institutions, groups, and factories of the people of the county, and compile statistics as a reference and preparation for promoting party affairs work. Secondly, to promote the doctrine of the party, it is also necessary to examine the general rural masses who do not know the principles of the party clearly and have not paid attention to the seven movements and local autonomy. Therefore, this outline has been specially formulated and the methods of implementation have been defined to provide guidelines for party members' work. Thirdly, for the training of party members, five articles of measures for training party members are specified in the plan, and the thinking and actions of party members are assessed at any time, and the party members are effectively guided and corrected. Fourthly, promoting social undertakings such as the equipment and promotion of various public undertakings and cooperative undertakings, promoting the expansion of local education, improving local customs and habits, and assisting the development of rural undertakings. The above four sections are the minimum limit in the promotion of party affairs in the county from today, and I hope to encourage all comrades in the county to do so. Fourthly, promote the realization of the new county administration. The General Manager stipulated in the Founding Program that the county is a unit of autonomy, and local autonomy is the only important work during the period of political tutelage. Returning to the oath of citizens in this county, although it has been held, the land in the county has not been completely measured, and the household registration survey is still waiting for accurate statistics. The establishment of schools has not been popularized, and the handling of the police is not perfect. The construction of county roads has not achieved much. All these are important items for autonomy. We people only recognize the observation of the current phenomenon as the beginning of the earth. To achieve the merit of nine piles, we still need the joint efforts of all people in the county. Based on the above points, for foreign countries, the unequal treaties should be abolished and imperialism should be overthrown. For internal affairs, peaceful unification should be supported to relieve the suffering of the people. Locally, the new county administration should be promoted and the county's autonomy should be completed. I hope that all the people and comrades of the county will work together with one heart and one mind to achieve success. This is the statement.

Having Gone Through All Kinds of Hardships

Many Excellent Photos Taken

Regular Public Exhibition This newspaper's special correspondent, Riverside photographer Wang Xiaoting and Liu Shuofu, went to Sichuan last year and went through the western Sichuan, southern Sichuan, and northern Sichuan areas. The Riverside Survey Staff Specially Sent by This Newspaper Returned to Shanghai (Photo Taken by This Newspaper) 160

Films of the various barbarian peoples have been successively published in this newspaper's pictorial section. Now, after passing through the Three Gorges to Yichang, the two gentlemen took the Pinghe Wheel and arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon. The families of the two gentlemen and their colleagues from this newspaper were there to greet them at the Yangshupu Wharf. The two gentlemen were in good spirits, but their faces were slightly dark due to the sun and wind. In addition to their personal luggage, there were 14 boxes of collected products from the border area, which will be shipped from Chongqing in a few days. The trip totaled six to seven thousand miles and took more than 1,600 scenic photos and more than 6,000 feet of moving film, all of which are extremely rare to see outside. In addition to traveling by boat, the two gentlemen mostly walked, experiencing wind, frost, rain, snow, bandits, and dangers, but fortunately, they were safe and sound. Now, it is planned to organize various films and then exhibit them publicly, and show moving films to introduce the truth of the riverside.

Case of the Domestic Goods Mall's Closure 166

The matter of the domestic goods mall being ordered to close by the Shanghai Municipal Council has not been resolved despite negotiations convened by the Chinese directors and the City Chamber of Commerce. The negotiation committee of the mall has been discussing solutions for days, and the employees are also requesting relief from all sectors of society. The various situations yesterday are recorded separately below.

Report to the City Government: The mall yesterday submitted the full record of the negotiations at the Chamber of Commerce to the City Government for reference. The original report stated: "Regarding the matter of our mall being illegally closed by the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession on June 19th, and the losses suffered by the staff who were beaten and arrested, [we] should directly request relief according to the law, etc., as instructed by the City Government's Order No. 1350. It is evident that the City Government is concerned about the people's plight and sympathizes with the difficulties of businesses, leaving no detail unaddressed. On the 19th and 20th of this month, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce notified our mall to send five representatives to a temporary meeting with five Chinese and foreign directors of the Shanghai Municipal Council. No arguments were presented during the report. We hereby record the case and respectfully request your examination and swift and serious protest to protect national rights and truly benefit the people. Respectfully submitted to Shanghai Mayor Zhang."

Ministry of Industry's Reply: The Ministry of Industry yesterday replied to the Cosmetics Industry Association, stating: "We have received and read the telegram. This case was previously reported to the Ministry by the mall and the Shanghai Chinese National Products Maintenance Association, the National Products Factory Association, and the Federation of National Products Factories. On the 13th of this month, we consulted with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a serious protest and negotiation. We have now copied and sent the association's telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for filing and handling. Please be informed."

Letter from the Lawyers' Association: Li Shirui, Tan Yigong, and Lu Shaozong, the standing committee members of the Shanghai Lawyers' Association, wrote to the domestic goods mall yesterday, stating: "We are writing in response to your telegram of the grey day. We have learned with respect that after your mall moved to New World, it was suddenly closed by the Shanghai Municipal Council's police on the pretext that the entertainment section did not fully comply with the regulations. Our association is extremely indignant. New World has been an entertainment venue for many years. If it was deemed unsuitable, it should not have been allowed to exist in the first place. Your mall is still in its old form, and although there have been changes, they are unlikely to go beyond the scope of the past. The so-called non-compliance with the regulations is unfounded. Even if there are non-compliant areas, they should not involve the entire mall due to the entertainment. Furthermore, even if the Shanghai Municipal Council has a special view and believes that there is a violation of the regulations, it should request the court to approve it in accordance with the law. How can it act directly and arbitrarily? This kind of measure by the Council treats the mall's entertainment as if it were a current bandit. We cannot but recognize it as an extrajudicial act of violence based on impartial observation. We earnestly hope that your mall will resolutely not yield and negotiate based on reason and law. Our association will do its best to support you."

Declarations from Various Places: The Hankou City National Products Movement Committee, the Henan Provincial National Products Factory Federation, the Qingdao National Products Movement Committee, the Coarse Cloth Industry Association, the Silk Weaving Industry Association, and other groups yesterday issued declarations and telegraphed the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government's various Yuan and Bu, proposing serious negotiations and the abolition of consular jurisdiction and unequal treaties. Discussion on Cotton Improvement at the Yangsi Central University Plantation 172

The National Central University College of Agriculture's Yangsi Cotton Field has been established for over ten years. It has spared no effort in managing the cotton planting experiment. Therefore, it has gained the trust of local farmers. In order to increase improvement and collect materials for experimentation, a discussion on cotton improvement was held at the field at 1:00 PM on the 21st of this month. Those who attended on that day included City Government Committee member Chen Zixin, cooperative farmers from the area such as Ma Shusheng, Zhang Shaoqi, and Ma Yunsheng, cotton merchants such as Zhang Jinsang and Chen Lin苑, rural teachers from the area such as Yuan Songfeng, Xi Xiahu, and Chen Zhuxin, and Yu Jun from the Jiangsu Provincial Zhoupu Agricultural Field, totaling more than 50 people. Japan Thoroughly Restricts Summer and Autumn Silkworms 173

The Japanese government, due to the collapse of the silk market, has already issued orders to reduce the amount of ant eggs for this year's spring silkworms in order to adjust production. It is heard that it will also restrict summer and autumn silkworms. Local sericulture officials once held a meeting to decide on the following methods: (1) The amount of summer and autumn silkworms raised by silkworm farmers will be reduced by 30% compared to the average production of the previous three years. (2) The amount of common silkworm eggs used in the production of summer and autumn silkworm eggs in silkworm seed factories will be reduced by 30% compared to the average amount in the previous three years. (3) Silk manufacturers should understand the purpose of the above-mentioned adjustment of summer and autumn silkworm cocoon production and should not intentionally hinder the transfer of cocoons to people and other thorough methods of adjusting production. In order to thoroughly implement the above-mentioned resolutions, several methods of execution are planned as follows: (1) The Minister of Agriculture and Forestry will directly issue instructions to local governors on the adjustment of summer and autumn silkworm cocoon production. (2) The central government will distribute letters of advice on adjusting summer and autumn silkworm cocoons to the domestic sericulture industry in the name of five organizations related to the sericulture industry in order to implement it. (3) The prefectures and counties shall take appropriate measures for the adjustment of summer and autumn silkworm cocoon production in accordance with the instructions of the Minister of Agriculture and Forestry.

Transportation costs also allowed to be reduced by 30%. Weicheng Company has long been famous in the national silk fiber industry. Great Chang Wheel Arbitration Stalled 177

Letters from both sides. The issue of responsibility for the sinking of the Da Chang wheel by a collision is still awaiting the organization of an arbitration committee. However, the customs house, due to the obstruction of navigation caused by the sunken Da Chang wheel, is paying for the salvage at a cost of 77,000 yen per day, equivalent to more than 150,000 yuan in Chinese currency. The Da Hua Company, due to the relationship of arbitration responsibility, requires the customs house to temporarily suspend the salvage in order to avoid the obscuring of the real evidence. The customs house then asked experts to draw a picture of the accident for use as a basis for negotiation, but the Ping An Company opposed the invitation of experts as members of the organization of the arbitration committee, resulting in delays. The Da Chang Company specially wrote to the Shipping Association requesting fair handling. The Ping An's reply and the original letter from Da Chang to the Shanghai Shipping Association are recorded separately below. Ping An's reply states: "In response to your company's letter of the 8th of this month, we have learned that the explanation given in our company's previous letter regarding the identity of the representative was only for fear that one party might not understand it, so we stated it in advance to avoid misunderstandings from occurring at the last minute. Moreover, the most important staff member of the company is the manager, so asking the manager to attend in person is to show solemnity and is not intended to be a restriction. Now, after reading your letter, the interpretation of the representative is contrary to our company's opinion, and even changed the original agreement. In addition to wanting to appoint a representative other than the company's legal representative, it is also proposed to appoint a consultant lawyer. Our company finds it difficult to agree to this new proposal and hopes that the conditions will still be discussed and agreed upon in accordance with the original agreement and our company's previous letter. If there are any further changes, our company will not be responsible for the delay." Da Chang's letter to the Association reads: "Respectfully, the Da Chang wheel of our company was sunk by a collision, and the Ping An Company has long agreed that both parties should send responsible representatives to the Association to agree on an arbitration contract. It is found that the selection of this representative is the absolute freedom of each party, and the only requirement is that the person is competent and responsible. The Ping An Company has misinterpreted, far-fetched, and forcefully expressed its opinion. He suddenly sent a letter stating that the representatives of both parties are limited to managers. Our company replied with a letter detailing the reasons and interests, and argued that the issue of representatives is not limited to managers and that both parties should each send two representatives and one legal advisor to attend the meeting to sign the contract. After the reply, it was said that it had already admitted that the previous letter had been interpreted for the identity of the representative as a prior statement, and suddenly pointed out that our company's proposal was a change to the original agreement, and finally claimed that it was difficult to agree to this new proposal. The words are flickering and full of contradictions. After an investigation, there were only agreements on sending responsible representatives in the previous letters between the two parties, and there was absolutely no motion on whether the representatives were limited to managers and how many representatives there should be. The Ping An Company falsely claims to have changed the original agreement. If you mean that the Ping An's previous letter is considered to be the original agreement, then it is close to coercion and as arbitrary. And since it has repeatedly admitted that the interpretation is said to be an explanation, it is said to be a statement, can this kind of interpretation and statement be referred to as the original agreement between the two parties, which suddenly claims to be this new proposal. It seems that dreaming in such dreams and being engaged in business in advance will make our company unable to find a solution. The matter has to be respectfully sent to you for inspection. We have always looked up to your society as our industry's teacher, and we must have excellent insights and knowledge. We respectfully request that you evaluate our company's proposal. If you think it is meaningful, please forward the letter to the Ping An Company to persuade them to accept it. Otherwise, after the examination, the meeting will give a quantitative modification in order to make it as perfect as possible. It is also only to be ordered to pray for guidance."

Children's Hygiene Movement 179

Yesterday was the last day of the lantern parade. The China Child Welfare Association held the Children's Hygiene Movement lantern parade last night, which was the last day. The various situations yesterday are recorded as follows:

Arrangement in Pudong: The Children's Health and Medical Clinic on Meizhou Road, Yangshupu, arranged and displayed children's hygiene posters, slogans, hygiene movement photos, etc., yesterday, which were pasted on the four walls and arranged in a new manner.

Infant Children: A kindergarten has been established on the upper floor of the Health and Medical Clinic, and Ms. Wang Aitian is in charge of everything. The room is surrounded by children's beds with bedding. There are more than ten small square tables, several small chairs, and a children's toy cabinet. Many children's hygiene pictures are hung on the walls. There are fifteen children in the room, ranging in age from two to five or six years old. Some are sleeping in bed, and some are playing various games. These children are the children of male and female workers in the factories of Shanghai Pudong. Because they have to go to work in the factory during the day and have no time to take care of them, they are sent to the garden for nurturing. The factory workers send them there at 6:30 in the morning, and the garden provides breakfast and lunch. The workers pick them up at 5:00 or 6:00 in the evening. Children of older age are also taught kindergarten readers and pictures for children to appreciate every day. The daily time is about three quarters of an hour.

Opening Ceremony: Yesterday, the venue was located in the Shanghai Pudong Public Society next to the Health Care Center. The opening ceremony was held at 7:00 PM. Luo Yunyan, the chairman, gave the opening remarks. Representatives from the City Party Headquarters, the Social Affairs Bureau, the Health Bureau, the Public Security Bureau, the Education Bureau, and other bureaus gave opinions on paying attention to children's health. Then, the children present sang the hygiene song.

Final Parade: Last night was the day of the children's lantern parade in Shanghai Pudong, which was also the last day of the parade. Children from various schools gathered one after another at the open space east of the Shanghai Pudong Public Society after 6:00 PM, lining up with about 500 people. The front of the team was the military band of the orphanage, and other children held lanterns, flags, and square lanterns. The parade set off after 6:00 PM, going south on Meizhou Road, Yangshupu, turning west to Taopeng Road, turning north into Pingliang Road, and then circling Yangshupu to the original place where the team was dismissed.

Evening Entertainment at the Venue: After 8:00 PM last night, students from the Ciyou Education Institute performed a new hygiene play in the Shanghai Pudong Public Society called "The Old Matchmaker of Diseases." The drama performed by the Youth Propaganda Group was called "Saving Our Children." At the end, a children's hygiene film was shown, and the audience did not leave until 11:00 PM.

Health Examination: The Shanghai Pudong Ciyou Health and Medical Clinic continued to hold a children's health competition today. The Public Concession Health Department and the City Health Bureau sent doctors to the hospital to give vaccinations to visitors, passersby, and those coming and going to the hospital.

New Developments in the Xin Kang Collision Case 182

The case of the China Merchants Bureau's Xin Kang steamer being sunk by the Japanese ship Ryuya Maru has been ongoing for nearly two years with no progress in negotiations. After the bereaved family association hired Wu Jingxiong and Sheng Zhenwei as legal counsel and litigation agents, all legal matters were fully prepared by the two lawyers. However, due to the large number of bereaved family members and their different places of origin, the procedures for entrusting the lawyers were delayed and could not be completed. As a result, the litigation has not made active progress. Recently, the bereaved family association published an advertisement to notify families who have moved or whose whereabouts are unknown to report to the association within a deadline. In recent days, the families have been reporting to the association one after another. There are a total of 205 victims, all of whom have signed letters of authorization entrusting the two lawyers to immediately file a lawsuit in the Shanghai Special District Court to request a judgment ordering compensation for damages. The bereaved family association has held many meetings to discuss all proceedings and has made concrete decisions. In recent days, they have been extremely busy handling various matters. It is said that the two lawyers are determined to fight for the case in accordance with the law because it concerns national rights and the lives of the people. The resolution of this long-dormant case is not far off.

Municipal Detective Team Cracks Kidnapping Case in Wuxing 185

Bandit Leaders Li Zhengpeng and Liu Shoushan

Female Hostage and Young Hostage Rescued. The Municipal Public Security Bureau's detective team cracked a major kidnapping case yesterday in Rongfuli, Gansi East Road, Xixiansi Road, French Concession, in which the victims were kidnapped from Wuxing County and hidden in Shanghai. A total of five male and female kidnappers were arrested, and one adult female hostage and one young child hostage were rescued on the spot. The details are as follows:

Secret Tip-Off Leads to Arrest 186

Lu Ying, captain of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's detective team, received a secret tip-off the day before yesterday (the 21st) stating that the notorious kidnappers Li Zhengpeng, Liu Shoushan, and Tang Zuo were responsible for kidnapping several hostages from the countryside in Wuxing County around February of this year. They had traveled by waterway via Taihu Lake to Shanghai and were currently hiding with the hostages at No. 17 Rongfuli, Gansi East Road, Xixiansi Road, French Concession. The tipster urged the team to dispatch officers immediately to arrest them and prevent them from escaping. Upon receiving the report, Captain Lu personally led team leader Shan Bin, Qi Haitian, detectives Chen Caifu, Yang Gussen, Zhou Peisan, Li Xiaobao, Shen Ruifu, Ling Tianpeng, Zhang Ruizhi, Deng Qishan, Zhang Yingpin, Wu Kezhong, Han Jingxiang, Liu Enyu, Xuanyuan Zhong, secret agents Shen Wenda, Zhao Huairen, and others, along with the informant, in several cars around 10 p.m. the previous evening.

Waiting According to Mr. Cai's Information 187

Captain Lu and his large group of detectives first went to the special agency of the French Concession police station, where they met with Western detective Bardi and Chinese and Western police officers. They proceeded to the address, but the bandits had already fled after hearing the news. However, all the items in the house had not yet been moved, so it was assumed that they had not gone far. Detective Zhang Ruizhi was assigned to wait in the house and questioned the landlord, Mr. Cai, who said that they had indeed left not long ago. Captain Lu ordered detectives Shen Wenda and Shen Ruifu to lie in wait at another location used by the bandits, No. 18 Zhenxingfang, on the same road.

Female Hostage Identifies Kidnappers 188

At around 6 a.m. yesterday, a man and a woman suddenly appeared at No. 17 Rongfuli. Upon seeing the detectives, they looked panicked. The man turned around and ran away. Detective Zhang Ruizhi ordered someone to guard the woman while he chased after the fleeing man. He pursued the man all the way to Remi Road, where he joined forces with the local police to intercept him. He was taken to No. 17, where the landlord identified him as the person who had come to rent the house. The arrested woman claimed that she was a hostage kidnapped from Wuxing, and the arrested man was one of the bandits, Liu Shoushan.

Kidnapped Sister-in-Law by Mistake 189

Detective Zhang then brought the two to Captain Lu for questioning. The female hostage stated her name was Zhang Shen, 23 years old, and she lived in Siqian Village outside the South Gate of Wuxing County. Her husband, Zhang Aman (25 years old), was a farmer. The family had a few acres of land, barely enough to make ends meet. In February of this year, she went to her mother's home in Shenjiahui, Wuxing, to visit her parents and her elder brother and sister-in-law. Her brother's name was A Long (26 years old), and his family also had good land and some savings. This time, the bandits had a dispute with A Long and intended to kidnap his wife, but she happened to be attending a gathering in a neighboring village, so they kidnapped me, my seven-year-old nephew Changshan, and my four-month-old baby.

Kidnappers Regret After Getting Money 190

After we were kidnapped, we first traveled by boat through Taihu Lake for two months. We finally arrived in Shanghai on April 22. The bandits initially demanded 1,500 yuan from my brother, promising to release all three of us. Unexpectedly, after my brother paid the bandits 1,500 yuan, they only released my nephew Changshan, and I and the baby continued to live in the bandits' den. Now, the bandits plan to extort a higher price from my husband's family, but my husband's family is very poor and cannot afford it, so they have no choice but to ignore it and leave it to fate.

Liu Shoushan Reveals Young Hostage 191

Upon questioning, the bandit Liu Shoushan stated that he was 48 years old, from Shandong, and worked as a cart pusher. He also revealed that there was a four-month-old hostage hidden in Room 6 of the Shunhe Hotel on Beile Road, Xujiahui, and he also revealed the location of his accomplices. Captain Lu ordered the original detectives to rush to Room 6 of the Shunhe Hotel, rescue the young hostage, and arrest the female bandit Zhang Wang, who was guarding the hostage. According to the hotel clerk, the bandits had rented six rooms: 1, 4, 5, 6, 7, and 8. While the team was interrogating them, the three bandits Tang Zuo, Li Zhengpeng, and Geng Fusheng were simultaneously apprehended at another bandit den at No. 18 Zhenxingli, Gansi East Road.

Director Chen Rewards Meritorious Service 192

The three newly captured bandits were interrogated strictly. Li Zhengpeng was the leader of the bandits, 57 years old, from Ningguo, Anhui. Tang Zuo stated that he was 33 years old, from Anhui. The female bandit Zhang Wang was 28 years old, from Shaoxing. The most surprising thing was that a Detective Symbol No. 92 of the Second District of the Zhejiang Inland River Water Police Bureau was found on the bandit Geng Fusheng. Geng claimed that he was 29 years old, from Guangshou, Henan, and had been working as a detective in the Water Police Bureau for only five days. After questioning, Captain Lu immediately reported the situation to Director Chen. Director Chen was very pleased and immediately approved a commendation for Captain Lu, noting a major merit. Team leader Shan Bin and Detective Zhang Ruizhi were each noted with one merit, and the remaining fourteen detectives, including Chen Caifu, were commended in advance and would be rewarded after the case was tried and judged. It is reported that Director Chen has specially dispatched officers to Wuxing County to notify the hostage families to come to Shanghai to identify them so that they can be reunited with their families as soon as possible.

Gujia Town Militia Cracks Kidnapping Case 193

Rescues Three Male and Female Hostages. The Gujia Town (formerly Gujiazai) militia, located in Baoshan County, cracked a bandit ship around 9 p.m. the night before last near the Yunzaobang Tang Bridge, about two miles east of the town. At that time, two bandits were captured, and three male and female hostages were rescued. The next morning, another accomplice bandit was captured and escorted to the Baoshan County government for interrogation. The details are as follows:

The Process of Cracking the Bandit Ship 194

Around 9 p.m. the night before last, militia chief Shen, deputy chief Gu, and Jia chiefs Li and Wang received a phone call from the Dachang militia reporting that a bandit ship with a pointed bow and copper railings had sailed towards Tang Bridge and requesting an immediate investigation. After receiving the report, the militia immediately ordered the platoon leaders to lead the militia members, led by the chief, deputy chief, and Jia chiefs, to set out in shifts to investigate. Near Tang Bridge, they saw a Jiangbei thatched boat parked in the river (this was another bandit ship, not the one with copper railings). They called out to it, but there was no response. The militia members became even more suspicious and fired several warning shots. A bandit peeked out and told the militia members that there was a patient on board. Then, a male hostage also peeked out and said, "I'm sick, I'm sick!" However, he kept gesturing to the militia members with his hands, so the militia members knew something was wrong and ordered him to come closer. They immediately boarded the ship and found two female hostages in the stern cabin. After questioning, they confirmed that they were kidnapped and rescued the three male and female hostages, along with the two bandits on board, and took them to the district militia.

Statements of Male and Female Hostages 195

The male hostage, Wu Songqin, 47 years old, from Qingpu County, a farmer, stated that he was kidnapped on the evening of the ninth day of the lunar month. His body was covered in cuts and bruises, and his hands and feet were tied with hemp rope, which may have caused permanent damage. He said that he tried to escape somewhere and jumped into the river, but the bandits noticed and dragged him up and beat him, so he was covered in mud. The militia provided him with newly made short shirts and trousers and ordered him to change. One of the female hostages was Xu Wu, 33 years old, whose husband's name was Xu Liukui, living in Zhangpu, Kunshan. The other female hostage, Yueqin, was Wu's daughter, 16 years old. Wu took Yueqin back to her mother's home in Shipu on the evening of the ninth day of the lunar month and was kidnapped by bandits. At the same time, Wu's cousin, Wu Xuezhou, was also kidnapped by bandits. However, Xuezhou was redeemed for 3,000 yuan at the end of April and is now overseas. The bandits want her and her daughter to pay 17,000 yuan to be redeemed.

Confessions of Bandits 196

One bandit, Tang Shaolian (aka A Da), 32 years old, a road worker, stated that Xue Renjie, Jiang Asan, Wu Asi, etc., had hired him to be a kidnapper. Xue Renjie is an old bandit with many handguns and submachine guns. He must go to Kunshan tomorrow (i.e., yesterday) wearing a black silk long shirt. He is a large man with pockmarks on his face. There is a Sanfengyuan teahouse inside the white powder wall at No. 7, west of the Zhonghua Paint Factory in Tanzikou, Zhabei, Shanghai. Zhou Ermazi, A Xiang, Wang Jinzhao, Xue San, etc., are all old bandits and live in Liudaoai, Yijiaojiao, near the Sun Temple (aka Xiao Erzi), 27 years old, a rickshaw puller, living in a straw shed behind the Fuxing Flour Mill in Xiaoshadu, Zhabei, along with Xue Renjie, Gao Laoda, A Er, Wang Youfa, Du Xiaosanzi, etc., more than 20 people. They all meet in the small teahouse in Tanzikou. I have only done this business twice. Last time, we went to Shihetang, Jiaxing, with 40 people and kidnapped three men and one woman and hid them in the west end of Caojiadu. One man was redeemed for 2,500 yuan overseas in December last year. There are more than 30 firearms. The newly captured bandit, Yan Zhiqing (aka Yan Asi), 29 years old (the above three bandits are all from Yancheng), came to look for the ship today and was arrested. There are five people on the ship. He also hired Xue Renjie to do this business. Xue runs the Sanfengyuan teahouse and sells wine and cigarettes. He also provided the names of the accomplices on the ship and the hostages, which were all the same. He also said that in November last year, he did two kidnapping cases near Kunshan. One time, he received 2,000 yuan, and he received 100 yuan. The other time, he received 4,000 yuan, and he received 200 yuan. The first time, there were 31 people, and there were more than 10 firearms. Now, all the firearms are with Gao Laoye. This time (referring to the current case of the kidnapped men and women), Xue Renjie, Tang Youfa, Zhou Ermazi, A Er, A Da, Xue Acai, Gao Laoda, Xue Er, Xue San, Liu Xiao Erzi (i.e., Daoai), Tang Asan, Qu San, Gu Zhiqing, a total of 13 people, went together. After verifying the confession, the militia sent Tang Shaolian and Liu Daoai, who were captured the night before last, to the county government for trial, and Yan Zhiqing was also sent to the county government for joint trial. It is understood that the county government has issued an order to the families of the hostages Wu Songqin, Xu Wu, and Xu Yueqin to be returned to the militia to be claimed by their families, so they have sent people to notify the families of the hostages.

Bad Weather, Many Patients 197

Doctors are Busy. Since the beginning of summer in this city, the weather has been abnormal, with clouds and rain one after another, and the temperature has been erratic. As a result, epidemics are prevalent. The health authorities are making every effort to carry out epidemic prevention work. In the Chinese area, doctors from the Health Bureau are leading students in teams to promote and inject preventive vaccines. In the concession area, health vehicles are also dispatched to various street corners to inject preventive vaccines for people, with hundreds of people being vaccinated every day. However, recently, the climate has been cold and hot, and residents are prone to infection if they are not careful about their diet and living habits. Wet-heat syndrome is the most common. Many children suffer from measles and chickenpox. Pediatricians and internists are very busy with outpatient and home visits.

Divorce Claiming Alimony 198

Li Fengzhu vs. Wang Caiming

Mediation Fails, Lawsuit Filed. Wang Caiming, a native of Yongxingli 153, Yuezhou Road, married Li Fengzhu from the same hometown. However, their relationship was not harmonious, and they often quarreled. Two years ago, Li sued him for assault, and the court sentenced him to a fine of 30 yuan, suspending the sentence for two years due to his first offense. Since then, she has returned to her mother's home at 1045 Dingheli, Yangshupu Road, for two years. Wang has also not come to welcome her back. They are nominally husband and wife, but in reality, they are like strangers. Li is only 22 years old and still young. If this continues, the happiness of her youth will be sacrificed. Recently, she has resolutely advocated divorce to avoid wasting her life. She filed a lawsuit with the Special District Local Court, requesting a preliminary mediation, demanding that Wang repay the loss of dowry, etc., 3,258.7 yuan, and alimony of 15,000 yuan, and that the marital relationship be dissolved. The requested alimony is calculated at 40 yuan per month, from the age of 22 to 60. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhou Daren of the Special Court held a court session for mediation, but Wang Caiming did not attend. Lawyer Yan Hongshih represented him in court and said that Wang could agree to Li's request for divorce, but the amount of alimony she wanted was too large for Wang to afford. If it were 300 or 500 yuan, he could consider it. Li said that Wang had assets of more than 100,000 yuan and that the Yongxingli residence where she now lives is his property, and he can afford the amount she is asking for. Judge Zhou asked if she could compromise, but she firmly refused. On the other hand, he was unwilling to provide a large amount of money, so mediation could not be effective. Judge Zhou instructed them to withdraw and asked Li to formally file a lawsuit to await trial.

Wei was from Henan and had served as a county magistrate. After resigning, he brought his wife to Shanghai to find work but failed. He attempted suicide in Pudong. His weak wife and young children have already passed away, and now Wei has committed suicide and died, which is truly sad.

Female Corpse Stealing Beans in Xiaohang, Pudong 201

Bean Loser is Suspected.

False Report by Landlord Detained. There is a Xiaohang in Yangjing East South, Pudong, which is a ditch shared by Chen Jinsheng and Xu Shunsheng for water use. The day before yesterday, a female corpse was found in the Hang. Wang Xiangchun, from Yancheng, went to identify the body and said that his wife, Zhou, 35 years old, had gone out to pick up firewood after lunch on the 17th of this month. The workers watching the corpse, Yang Nengxi and Xu Shaokui, suddenly said that the corpse was beaten to death for stealing beans. Wang Xiangchun was unwilling to give up after hearing this and filed a complaint with the Third District Police Station. The police were dispatched to investigate and found broad beans next to the corpse, which clearly indicated that beans had been stolen. Upon further investigation, it was found that Chen Jinsheng had beanstalks planted on his land. When asked, Chen Jinsheng admitted that he had a lot of broad beans stolen. However, the police did not know how the corpse died and how it was found. The police suspected that Chen Jinsheng and Shunsheng were involved and arrested them. Xu claimed that his family had not had any beans stolen and did not know where the corpse came from. Since Yang Nengxi and others had said that the deceased was beaten to death, they must know the reason, so they were also detained for questioning. They did not admit anything, so the 47th Tu landlord, Lu Jinquan, was ordered to report to the Local Court for examination. However, the landlord reported that she had drowned. Yesterday, Prosecutor Wu and examiners came to the scene to examine the corpse and found that the corpse had a fatal injury to the head and was thrown into the Hang after death. The Hang was only half a foot deep, so how could it drown someone? Therefore, he ordered the body to be buried, and the corpse's husband went to the station to accuse the landlord of concealing the matter for many days without reporting it. Therefore, the station detained the landlord and sent him to the Local Court for custody and investigation.

Oar Rope Breaks, Boatwoman Wu Bochen 202

Yang Asan, from Jiangbei, has been making a living by rowing boats. His wife, Hu, 23 years old, is from the same hometown as Yang. The couple lives on the boat and makes a living by transporting light cargo. At noon yesterday, Yang first rowed the boat alone from Longmao Wharf in Lujiazui, Pudong, to Puxi. When they reached the center of the river, his wife helped him row the oars. Unexpectedly, the oar rope suddenly broke, and Hu fell into the river. Yang jumped down to save her but was unable to reach her, and she drowned and disappeared. Yang was devastated and reported to the Water Police Station for record.

Fake Refined Talk Costs a Life 203

Sister Cannot Tolerate Sister's Anger

Invoice Indirectly Kills. The woman Miao Chen, 28 years old, who lives at 516 Zhejiang Road, received an invoice from the rice shop for rice on the Dragon Boat Festival in the lunar calendar. Her sister said that she did not recognize the words, so why pretend to be refined? They quarreled, and she took a lot of opium and committed suicide. Her mother, Miao Zhao, returned home and noticed it. She was sent to the hospital for treatment, but it was too late, and she died. The police station in charge reported the matter and sent the corpse to the Feilun Road examination office. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo of the Special Court came to the office to examine the body and ordered Miao Zhao to sign a guarantee to claim the body for burial.

Nurse Commits Suicide at Tongren Hospital 204

Fu Xing (20 years old), a nurse from Fujian at Hongkou Tongren Hospital, committed suicide by taking morphine for unknown reasons around 2 a.m. the night before last. Lou Qinglin, who lived in the same room, was awakened from his dream by his groans and went to check on him. Fu's face turned pale, and he knew something was wrong. He asked him, but he did not answer, so he ran to tell the doctor, Pan Zhongyi, who came to rescue him, but it was too late. He then reported to the Hongkou police station, who ordered detectives to investigate and sent the corpse to the Feilun Road examination office. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo Wei of the Special District Local Court came to the office to examine the corpse and held a public hearing. According to the testimony of Lou Qinglin, the deceased was very kind and did not waste money. He did not know the reason for his suicide. Prosecutor Guo obtained the confession and ordered that the corpse be examined and confirmed that Fu Xing had committed suicide by taking poison. The corpse was handed over to Pan Zhongyi for burial.

Due to a Trivial Matter of Not Returning Borrowed Clothes. Xia Xigen, 25 years old, a worker in the lead printing department of the Commercial Press, was stabbed three times with a sharp knife by his younger brother, Xia Jingen, at the Yang Yongtai Hotel in Zhabei around 7 p.m. yesterday. The police officers of the Third Section of the Fifth District Public Security Bureau arrived at the scene and arrested the murderer and took him to the station for investigation. The reason for the murder was that he had been holding a grudge for not being able to borrow clothes.
